Current Affairs Commentary

Seeing off the Old Year and Welcoming in the New. 27

Time flies like an arrow. In the blink of an eye, there is only one day left of the 21st year of the Republic of China. Looking back on the past year, let us carefully examine the progress of our country's politics, the progress of our economy, and how much the vitality of our people has increased. The deeper the recognition, the more we cannot help but feel sadness, and the more urgent our inspiration.

Since the September 18th Incident of the year before last, our country has been in a position of inferiority and defeat everywhere. We lost Shenyang and Jilin without a fight. When the enemy launched a sudden attack, we abandoned Jinzhou. Although China has vast lands, how many times can it withstand being divided and carved up? The only thing that can be comforting is that after the Shenyang Incident, the people had a slight motivation to improve, and the government also had the determination to make a fresh start with the people. The party and state elders also strongly advocated "spiritual solidarity to jointly face the national crisis." The previous disharmony was completely eliminated due to the great disaster. From then on, we could unite from top to bottom and the whole country could work together to face the national crisis. Who knew that the January 28th Incident would suddenly erupt in our armpit? Shanghai, the national center of finance and industry, was bombarded. Only the capital, Nanjing, was spared. The war lasted for thirty-two days. From the perspective of sorrow and depression, the prosperous area of Zhabei was reduced to scorched earth. The strategically important land of Wusong suddenly became a field of rubble. Considering only the tangible material losses in the Shanghai and Wusong area, it should be over 100 million yuan. And the spiritual losses, the cost of lives, and the indirect losses of all industries in the southeast region are not included. The loss of the Northeast is truly a national humiliation that our people will never forget. The bloodshed in Shanghai is an even deeper hatred that our nation will never forget for a hundred years. However, on the other hand, although our country has suffered unprecedented difficulties and is in a time when all industries are declining and the countryside is extremely exhausted, we can still barely support ourselves. With only a small force, we are facing the enemy of the entire country.

For more than a month of war, the general public exerted their spirit of diligence and hard work to assist the government, resist strong enemies from abroad, and suppress chaos from within. Although it was impossible to accomplish everything perfectly in such a short period of time, the national spirit has been fully demonstrated. Having understood the way to self-reliance and recovery, how can we count the achievements of one day for an ancient country with five thousand years of deep-rooted habits? Moreover, with a strong enemy in front and the national crisis being urgent, there are still areas that need to be cleaned up.

In today's world, it is not only our country that is loudly proclaiming national crisis. With the wealth of the United States of America, whether it is natural resources or human labor, it can be called the world's leader since the European War. However, since the economic panic occurred, it has gradually declined. In June 1931, President Hoover announced the postponement of indemnity and war debt payments, fully expecting that the world economy would have a turning point. However, a year and a half has passed, and the world economy has not improved. On the contrary, the situation in the United States has become even more panicked. Industrial manufactured goods are piled up like mountains. Wheat and cotton have also fallen to the lowest value required for production costs. Goods are congested and cannot be sold, while the number of unemployed has increased (to over ten million). Starving people are everywhere. Germany, with its tightly organized structure and strong spirit, is in an extremely difficult situation, both politically and economically, due to heavy oppression. The Brüning cabinet maintained the smooth operation of its national economy through emergency decrees. When Papen came to power, it was almost an absolute autocracy. Although he had dissolved the parliament, he could not win a majority of seats, surpassing the fascist movement of the Hitler Party. By the time General Schleicher formed a cabinet, combining the positions of Prime Minister and Minister of Defense, it was purely a military government. However, can the current economic difficulties of Germany be solved by military force? Over five million unemployed workers (according to a trade union survey, complete unemployment accounts for 47% of the 20.75 million workers). Is this kind of scene lighter than war? Among the European countries, France has the most stable economic situation. In fact, its peak of prosperity came later than other countries, so its decline is also later. Moreover, it has received a large amount of indemnity. Since last year, although it has tried its best to increase tariff barriers, import trade has decreased as a result, and export trade has also decreased by more than 30% compared to last year. The number of unemployed workers has suddenly increased to 340,000. The national treasury expenditure has increased by 50% compared to 1926. Therefore, France, which has abundant gold reserves and ranks second in the world, still has its economic crisis continuing. Britain was originally the leader of capitalist countries. Since the autumn of last year, it has abandoned its gold standard and willingly relinquished its financial throne, using inflation policies to maintain its declining economy. An advanced constitutional country has even deviated from the normal path of constitutionalism and organized a national unity cabinet to deal with its extraordinary (national crisis). 2.92 million unemployed people are still unable to find employment. Japan believes that its military sword can conquer everything and that military victory can eliminate the current predicament. It does not know that increased military spending is the only obstacle to the recovery of the market. If China refuses to yield, then Japan's so-called national crisis will never be resolved.

Looking around the world today, small countries aside, all are collapsing on the road to bankruptcy. Even the so-called six major powers are all in the midst of crisis. All are exerting their full strength, either based on their own country, such as the British Empire's economic alliance, or with the goal of expanding territory, such as Japan's invasion of our country. But the one thing they have in common is the whole country going crazy to face the national crisis.

Looking back at our country, from the September 18th Incident to the January 28th Incident, the people of our country were under the oppression of a strong enemy's violence, but they were still able to help themselves with great effort, seize the opportunity to rise up, and suddenly there was a new atmosphere of China's recovery. How long has it been? The crisis in front of us remains the same. The three northeastern provinces have fallen into the hands of the enemy. The wounds of the Shanghai war have not yet healed. The enemy's troops are flaunting their power in our country. And the general public, after a period of relaxation (the countryside has seen a slight harvest, but industry and commerce are trapped in the cities), are turning a blind eye to the current crisis, singing and dancing, drunk and dreaming, only seeking momentary pleasure and happiness, waiting for the enemy to perish on their own, and ignoring the fall of the Northeast. They have no regard for the future of the nation and the country. They do not even know to be vigilant when danger is at hand. What is even worse is that they are not satisfied with harming themselves, but instead blame the local area, inflict disasters on the people, and give the enemy an excuse to laugh at friendly countries, leaving shame for the world and putting the country in danger. Therefore, those who love us stand by and watch, those who hate us kick us when we are down, and those who hate us even wield the knife to cut us.

From the publication of the League of Nations' investigation report to the meeting of the League of Nations' Administrative Council, in these three months, looking at our country, the conflict between Han Fuju and Liu Zhennian was fortunately quelled, but the fighting between the two Lius in Sichuan even involved the use of land, sea, and air forces. The innocent people of Sichuan had to endure the cruel disaster as if they were in an enemy country. Before the Sichuan war was over, there was the struggle between the Qian army and You Guocai. Even Guizhou, which is as barren and bitter as Guizhou, could not avoid repeated military disasters. The hard-working farmers who are loyal to their work, even if they use all their strength, can hardly get a moment of peace. The Yangtze River Delta area suffered from floods last year, and the houses were empty. This spring, they suddenly heard about the Shanghai war and were terrified. The autumn harvest was once again a disaster due to cheap grain. Life is as thin as a thread. What we rely on for support is the historical virtue of perseverance and hard work of our people to prop up this precarious situation. Therefore, the enemy country is trying every means to bully us and mocking us in every way. They even say that our country is an unorganized country. Their intention is to imply to the powers from the root that "China has not yet formed a modern country, so it can be taken at will." They are also strengthening their military preparations. During the League of Nations' General Assembly, they also used the name of troop rotation to transfer the Kumamoto 6th Division to the Jinzhou and Yi County area, preparing to take the opportunity to invade Rehe and seize Shanhaiguan. The international alliance that advocates peace is not only influenced by the two major powers of Britain and France to maintain the balance of power in Europe, but is now also deliberately accommodating Japan, implementing delays and watching, allowing the peace of East Asia to be shattered under the iron hooves of Japanese militarism.

From now on, the Eastern market will lose its balance. The roots of war are being planted deeper and deeper. The war-mongering Japanese warlords are wielding their military swords and criticizing peace, even wanting to settle accounts with our country.

Our country is in this dangerous environment and is facing an incomparably strong and stubborn enemy. We must rise up and fight in time, fight flesh and blood, and work together to win the final victory against the enemy. Although our strength is weak, if we do our best to fight Japan, the final victory will surely belong to "the one who is grieved." On this New Year's Eve, I hope that the people of the country will strive to encourage themselves. "All things of the past are like yesterday's death. All things of the future are like today's birth!"

○ ○ ○ ○ ○ ○ ○

The Earthquake in Gansu Was Extremely Severe, with the Epicenter in the Tianshan Mountains 28

Remarks by Researchers at the Academia Sinica

(Nanjing) The earthquake in Gansu this time was extremely severe. According to a researcher at the Meteorological Research Institute of the Academia Sinica, the Gansu earthquake occurred at 10:08:54 AM on the 25th of this month. Nanjing felt the tremor four minutes after the earthquake occurred. The epicenter was in the Tianshan Mountains. The cause of the earthquake was the fault structure of the mountains. Therefore, the duration of the earthquake was more than two hours. Its severity even broke earthquake records, surpassing the tragedies of the Xinjiang-Gansu earthquakes in 1920 and 1927. The radius of the ground rupture was about 20 Chinese miles. Suzhou suffered heavy losses due to the impact of the epicenter wave. Other areas around the epicenter, such as Lanzhou, Qinghai, Mongolia, and Sichuan, were also affected by aftershocks. In addition to notifying the meteorological observatories in Shanghai, Beiping, Soviet Russia, the Dutch East Indies, and India, the Meteorological Research Institute is also paying attention to reporting to each other. Furthermore, since the earthquake occurred in Xinjiang in the northwest last year, and this year it has moved east and west to Gansu, another earthquake has occurred. The cause will be carefully studied in the future. (30th Dispatch)

It is heard that the remaining bandits have again dispersed and fled towards northern Sichuan. Our divisions under Liu Maoen, Xiao Zhichu, and Hu Zongnan are still pursuing them. The Sichuan, Shaanxi, and Hubei armies have decided to encircle and suppress them immediately, so as to eliminate them in one fell swoop. (30th Dispatch)

(Hankou) He Chengjun telegraphed the Suiyuan Pacification Headquarters on the 29th that the Xu bandits were defeated in southern Shaanxi and seemed to be fleeing to the border of Sichuan. The National Army is blocking them in the Shiquan and Ziyang area. The future of bandit suppression is optimistic. He will return to Hankou in about ten days. (30th Dispatch)

(Hankou) According to military sources, most of Xu bandits' remnants have fled into the northern part of Tongjiang and Nanjiang counties in northern Sichuan, near Yusi Pass. (30th Dispatch)

The Plan to Reduce the Number of Provinces Will Begin with Investigation 34

(Nanjing) A certain Central Committee member said that the size of our country's provinces is larger than that of a single European or American country, which is a major reason why politics is not easy to advance. The cultivation of warlords in the past was also conceived from this. Therefore, there are already many people who advocate reducing the number of provinces. Since the proposal was put forward and passed by member Wu Chao-shu at the Fourth Plenary Session of the Central Committee of the Kuomintang two years ago, it has aroused the attention of the people of the country and many have expressed their support. However, given the current situation, it is a difficult issue to implement. But the first step in this matter is to investigate the population, geography, economy, customs, transportation, etc. of each province, and at the same time solicit the opinions of experts, and then formulate detailed methods. As for the recruitment of talents for investigation, it is another major difficulty. It must take a long time to succeed. Moreover, Shi Ying proposed to change the provincial system, so that from now on, the powers will be concentrated in the hands of the governor. Judging from the past and present, if a governor does not have military power, can he fully exercise his duties? If he has military power, can he avoid repeating the abuses of military personnel governing in the past? In the future, if the number of provinces can be reduced and the provincial system can be changed, it will be most appropriate. The implementation of the above two plans must be complementary. The Central Political Council will first send them to the Economic and Legal Systems Groups to review them together, and then submit them to the Standing Committee for discussion to determine the principles and make practical preparations. If we want to implement them at the beginning of the constitutional government, we must proceed quickly at this time. (30th Dispatch)

Rizal Martyrdom Day: U.S. House Passes Philippine Independence Bill 77

With Looser Restrictions on Immigration and Trade

Advocating for the U.S. to Permanently Retain Naval and Military Powers

Filipinos Rejoice and the Entire Nation is Ecstatic

Manila, 29th (National News Agency): Today is the 36th anniversary of the martyrdom of Philippine independence fighter José Rizal. It is a legal holiday in the Philippines, and all sectors are taking a day off. The news of the U.S. Congress passing the independence bill has arrived here, making Filipinos even more joyful and the entire nation ecstatic. A large number of Manila citizens participated in a parade, departing from Rizal Street at 3 p.m., circling the entire city, and arriving at the Rizal Monument in Luneta Park in the evening for a grand review and speeches about Rizal's deeds before dispersing. Parades were also held throughout the island, with beauty pageants held in advance to select the most beautiful girl as the Rizal Day Queen, serving as the leader of the parade on this day. The participants competed in colorful and strange costumes to add to the parade's splendor. Apart from grand prayers held in various churches, the original intent of mourning had long been lost, turning into a festival of entertainment. However, today, as the freedom for which Rizal fought throughout his life is about to be realized, everyone feels joyful. Rizal was one of the greatest figures in the Philippines, also being a doctor, philanthropist, social reformer, poet, writer, and linguist. Although he advocated for peaceful reform throughout his life, the Spanish military authorities accused him of inciting revolution and brutally executed him by firing squad in Bagumbayan at 6 a.m. 36 years ago.

Washington, 29th (Havas): The draft law regarding the autonomy of the Philippine Islands was recently passed by the House of Representatives, stipulating that autonomous rights be granted to the Philippines after ten years.

Washington, 29th (National News Agency): The U.S. House of Representatives debated this bill for only one hour before passing it today, which is rare. This indicates that even if the bill is vetoed by President Hoover, there will still be enough votes to pass it again. Although there has been no record-breaking vote in the Senate, it is said that before the vote, no more than fifteen people actually opposed independence. It is expected that if a second vote is needed in the future, it may not be impossible to obtain the required two-thirds majority. The bill will now be signed by the Speaker of the House, Garner, and sent back to the Senate. After being signed by the President of the Senate, Vice President Curtis, it will be sent to the President. Hoover is currently out of the capital for fishing, and will likely return to the capital within the next week. According to the Constitution, he has several days to consider before either approving or rejecting it. However, even after the President approves it, the bill must be passed by the Philippine Legislative Assembly or Constitutional Convention before it takes effect.

Washington, 29th (Reuters): According to the compromise reached by the House of Representatives on the Philippine Independence Bill today, the joint committee of both houses drafted it. In addition to the independence clauses, it also contains milder restrictions on immigration and trade than before, and includes provisions advocating that the United States should permanently retain full naval and military power in the Philippines, and requesting the President to negotiate a treaty with foreign governments recognizing the Philippines' permanent neutrality upon its independence.

Manila, 30th (National News Agency): Philippine Senate President Quezon, a leader of the independence movement, assured today that the independence bill passed by the U.S. Congress, although containing some unsatisfactory provisions, can be accepted by the Philippines. He stated that considering the current situation in Washington, the bill may already be considered the best possible option. However, he intends to cable his representative in Washington to explain this situation, and that he personally will approach this bill with a very open mind, and will provide a detailed commentary after thorough study.

Amidst the Invasion of Jehol, the Japanese Exchange Rate Continues to Fall 78

The Bank of Japan Overissues Gold Notes, Setting a New Record

Cash Reserve is Only 29 Percent

Tokyo, 30th (China United News Agency): Yesterday, in the New York exchange market, the Japanese exchange rate fell another nineteen cents, closing at 20.81 cents. According to Japanese speculators, the exchange rate against foreign currencies will fall again in a month. They cited five reasons: (1) The Japanese fiscal future is becoming more pessimistic. During the ongoing congressional session, the shortcomings of Japanese finance will inevitably be gradually exposed to the world financial community, causing a decline in Japan's credit. (2) The control of the Dalian clique is ineffective. (3) The situation in the League of Nations remains sluggish, and the future is extremely worrying. (4) The military offensive against Jehol will begin in mid-January. If this war again provokes public outrage from world opinion, the situation will become unmanageable. (5) Japan's foreign trade has entered a period of excess imports. With the above reasons, the financial community in the new year will have difficulty recovering. Although military industries may slightly recover, the remaining foreign exchange from the reactionary boom, falling prices, and high prices will plunge the opinions of the working and peasant classes into poverty.

Tokyo, 30th (China United News Agency): According to a report by the Bank of Japan, the gold notes issued today reached 1,455,306,000 yuan, which is 29,992,000 yuan more than the previous record in 1916, and 74,140,000 yuan more than the same period last year. It can be said to be a new record since the founding of Japan. Its cash reserve of 425,068,000 yuan is only 29 percent.

Spanish Revolutionary Party's Conspiracy to Revolt Exposed 79

Barcelona, 30th (National News Agency): The three parts of the Spanish Revolutionary Party, namely the Industrial Revolutionary Party, the Anarchist Party, and the Communist Party, have recently abandoned their differences and conspired to revolt together. Fortunately, a bomb exploded in the old ammunition depot of party members in Barcelona, ​​which attracted the attention of the police, who seized a large amount of military equipment, such as bombs, hand grenades, rifles, pistols, and bullets, as well as many secret documents, and learned the location of arsenals and bomb depots throughout the city and elsewhere. The police authorities immediately went to each location and seized them with lightning speed. The party's plan was to take advantage of the public celebrating the New Year to distribute military equipment on Sunday morning, and agree to start the revolt at 10 a.m. Railway workers would also go on strike at that time to obstruct the movement of troops, because the party leaders knew that the garrison in Barcelona would be easily subdued if they could not get outside support. The party also relied on a part of the military to rebel against the government, because there were several officers on the roster. Fortunately, the discovery was made early, otherwise, it would have been difficult to manage.

Japan's Arrogance Grows Daily: War in North China is Inevitable 80

The Warning of the British Labour Party Newspaper

Those Who Promote Japanese Arrogance Should Bear Full Responsibility

At that time, China will no longer remain silent and will inevitably resist with arms, and a real war will begin from then on. Those who bear most of the responsibility for this war will be those who have now tacitly approved Japan's actions, causing its arrogance to grow daily.

Hoover and Roosevelt Disagree: U.S.-France Trade Agreement Negotiations Stalled 81

Washington, 29th (Havas): Secretary of State Stimson formally notified French Ambassador to the United States Claudel that U.S.-French trade negotiations have completely stopped. Regarding this matter, Under Secretary of State Castle made a correction, saying that the trade negotiations have not stopped, but only been temporarily suspended. Stimson and Claudel never discussed the U.S.-France trade agreement. President Hoover is about to leave office, and regarding international issues, he cannot take any measures in fact without first obtaining the consent of the new President Roosevelt. Roosevelt's views are completely different from Hoover's, especially regarding trade agreements and tariff issues. For example, Roosevelt advocates for reducing tariff rates, while Hoover advocates for raising them. Their opinions differ so much that Roosevelt, in order to preserve his freedom to negotiate after taking office, is unwilling to intervene in political affairs at this time.

Indictment of Chen Duxiu Case 83

Indictment from the Jiangsu High Court Prosecutor's Office

Chen and Ten Others Accused of Endangering the Republic of China

After Chen Duxiu, Peng Shuzhi, and others were escorted to Nanjing, the Ministry of Justice instructed the Jiangsu High Court to handle the case according to the law. Prosecutor Zhu went to Nanjing for investigation, which has now concluded. Except for Wang Xiaochun, for whom no substantial evidence was found and who will not be prosecuted, Chen Duxiu, Peng Shuzhi, Wang Wu, Pu Yifan, Wang Ziping, He Afang, Wang Zhaoqun, Guo Jinghao, Liang Youguang, and Wang Jiantang, a total of ten people, are deemed to have committed crimes endangering the Republic of China based on conclusive evidence and should be held criminally responsible. A public prosecution was filed with the Criminal Division of the same court the day before yesterday. As soon as President Lin returns to Suzhou (Lin is currently in Zhenjiang reporting on his work at the Jiangsu Provincial Representative Assembly), he will appoint a presiding judge to go to Nanjing to conduct the trial. The indictment of Prosecutor Zhu is excerpted below:

Defendants Chen Duxiu, Peng Shuzhi (also known as Zhang Cinan), Wang Wu (also known as Song Fengchun), Pu Yifan, Wang Yuping, He Afang, Wang Zhaoqun, Guo Jinghao (also known as Peng Daozhi), Liang Youguang, and Wang Jiantang, the above ten defendants, are all in custody. The above-mentioned defendants are involved in Case No. 38, Criminal Character, of the Republic of China, which endangers the Republic of China. The investigation has been completed, and it is deemed that a public prosecution should be filed. The criminal facts of the defendants and the articles of law violated are listed below:

In October of this year, the Shanghai Public Security Bureau received a tip that a counterfeit central organ of the Communist Party was located on the upper floor of No. 210 Chunyang Lane, Dongyouheng Road, in the Shanghai International Settlement. Inspector Tang Bao and Zhang Qingtai were secretly dispatched with a letter to the First Special District Court to issue a search and arrest warrant. They, along with Western Detective Gode and Western Detective Clerk Laosilai of the police station, went to the address at 3:00 PM on the 15th of the same month. Xie Shaoshan and the defendants Pu Yifan, Peng Shuzhi (also known as Zhang Cinan), Wang Wu (also known as Song Fengchun), and Wang Zhaoqun, five people in total, were holding their weekly meeting and were arrested together. A large number of reactionary documents were seized on the spot, along with several scraps of paper with communication addresses. Based on these addresses, detectives went to the upper floor of No. 11 Yongyu Lane, Yuezhou Road, at 7:00 PM on the same day and arrested the defendant Chen Duxiu, seizing a large number of reactionary documents. At around 9:00 PM, they searched Pu Yifan's residence at No. 322 Gaofu Lane, Shengmuyuan Road, and seized various reactionary documents, and also arrested Wang Xiaochun. At around 12:00 AM that night (the 16th, 0:00 AM), they went to No. 1044 Siwen Lane, Datong Road. Because it was late at night, the door was knocked on, and the people inside were frightened by the noise. Two people jumped out of the window, one escaped, and only the defendant Liang Youguang was arrested, and several reactionary documents were seized. At 7:30 AM, they went to the lower floor of No. 335 Yeguang Lane, Tangshan Road, where the defendants Wang Ziping and He Afang were printing communist publications "Spark" and "School Life," and they were arrested along with the evidence. At 12:00 PM, they went to No. 20 Fuli Lane and arrested the defendant Wang Jiantang, seizing ten types of reactionary books. Previously, after the detectives arrested Wang Ziping and others in the house at No. 335 Yeguang Lane, Tangshan Road, they immediately dispatched people to guard it secretly. On the 17th, the defendant Guo Jinghao (also known as Peng QiuZhi), unaware that the matter had been exposed, went to the house and was also arrested by the guarding police officers. They were then escorted to the Second Branch of the Jiangsu High Court and handed over to the Shanghai Public Security Bureau to be brought back. First, Chen Duxiu and Peng Shuzhi were transferred to the Military Law Department of the Army Headquarters of the Ministry of Military Administration. After questioning, it was determined that they were not related to the communist bandits in Hubei and Jiangxi, and Chen Duxiu and others were not active military personnel. Moreover, the location of the crime did not comply with the provisions of the first paragraph of Article 7 of the Emergency Law on Punishing Crimes Endangering the Republic of China. It was deemed that they had no jurisdiction and were transferred to this office by the Ministry of Justice for handling according to the law. This office collected the case files and interrogated them repeatedly. Chen Duxiu, Peng Shuzhi, and others admitted to joining the Communist Party, establishing the Left Opposition faction of the Chinese Communist Party, and being elected as members of the Central Publications Committee. During the investigation, it was discovered that the police of the Shanghai International Settlement had seized more than 40 types of reactionary documents in Chen Duxiu's home. Staff members were dispatched to the Central Party Headquarters to collect all the documents and the Shanghai Public Security Bureau subsequently delivered the accomplices Wang Wu (also known as Song Fengchun), Pu Yifan, Wang Ziping, He Afang, Wang Zhaoqun, Guo Jinghao, Liang Youguang, and Wang Jiantang, a total of nine people, to this office for joint trial. As a result of the investigation, except for Wang Xiaochun, for whom no substantial evidence was found and who will not be prosecuted, the criminal acts of Chen Duxiu and the other nine defendants should be discussed separately as follows:

(1) Chen Duxiu's Part: The defendant Chen Duxiu is from Huaining, Anhui. He initially studied at Tokyo University in Japan. He returned to China briefly during the first and second years of Xuantong in the Qing Dynasty (1909-1910) to engage in writing. After the restoration, he went to Japan again to continue his studies. In the fourth year of the Republic of China (1915), he returned to China and went to Shanghai, where he served as the editor of the Youth Magazine, aiming to oppose religion, warlords, and Confucianism. In the fifth year of the Republic of China (1916), he went to Peking University as the dean of the Faculty of Arts until the ninth year of the Republic of China (1920), when he returned to Shanghai to run the Youth Magazine. In the same year, he joined the Communist Party. He then went to Guangdong to serve as the Director of Education for about a year. He returned to Shanghai due to illness. In the eleventh year of the Republic of China (1922), he went to Moscow and stayed for about two months. After returning to China, he was appointed as the General Secretary of the Communist Party, directly receiving orders from Moscow and directing the activities of the Communist Party in various places. Until the sixteenth year of the Republic of China (1927), due to the Kuomintang's purge of the Communists and the failure of the Communist Party, the Third International dismissed him from his position as General Secretary, claiming he was ineffective in performing his duties. At that time, the Communist Party internally split into two factions: (1) the Stalin faction, also known as the Cadre faction; (2) the Trotsky faction. The defendant leaned towards the Trotsky faction and disagreed with the Cadre faction. By the second half of the eighteenth year of the Republic of China (1929), he was expelled from the party. Thereupon, the defendant gathered a group of expelled individuals, such as Peng Shuzhi, Wang Ziping, and Song Fengchun, and organized the Left Opposition faction of the Chinese Communist Party in Shanghai. The defendant and Peng Shuzhi and Zhang Jiu were elected as members of the Standing Committee of the Central Executive Committee, and Song Fengchun and Pu Yifan were elected as alternate members of the Standing Committee. They also established branches in Beijing, Tianjin, Guangzhou, Hong Kong, and other places to carry out activities separately. Due to limited funding, they only participated in labor unions and student movements, and because there were fewer party members in the farmers' associations, they could not expand. The party's publications included "School Life" and "Spark," both of which were edited by the defendant. All of the above facts were confessed by the defendant in the police station, the Second Branch of the High Court, and this office, and are consistent with the confessions of the accomplice Peng Shuzhi and others. The defendant is the chief of the Standing Committee of the Central Executive Committee of the Left Opposition faction of the Chinese Communist Party (hereinafter referred to as the CCP Opposition), and is the mastermind of a party. He should be responsible for his personal actions and the reactionary documents he published. Moreover, he should be fully responsible for the reactionary leaflets and manifestos published in the name of the CCP Opposition and the actions he directed. After reviewing the "Political Resolution on the Current Situation and Our Tasks" published in the name of the CCP Opposition (Evidence No. 24), the "Appeal to the People on the Seventh Anniversary of the May Thirtieth Movement" (Evidence No. 5), the "Declaration on the Current Situation" (Evidence No. 6), the "Notice of the Organizational Committee" (Evidence No. 10), the "Appeal to the People on the Japanese Imperialists' Recent Attack on Shanghai" (Evidence No. 11), the "Appeal to the People of the Whole Country on the Japanese Occupation of Shanghai" (Evidence No. 15), the "Appeal to the People by the Committee of the Eastern District of Shanghai on the Japanese Massacre in Shanghai" (Evidence No. 16), the "Appeal to the People of the Whole Country on the Japanese Occupation of Shanghai" (Evidence No. 20), and the "Recent Work Plan of the Beijing Special Committee" (Evidence No. 323), on the one hand, they used diplomacy as a pretext to vigorously promote communism; on the other hand, they coldly ridiculed and wantonly attacked the Kuomintang government. In essence, they claimed that the Kuomintang government's credibility had fallen to the ground and it could not lead the masses. They should lead the farmers, workers, and proletariat in armed uprisings, organize peasant-worker armies, establish a Soviet regime, overthrow the National Government, and implement a proletarian dictatorship, and wanted to overthrow capitalists, confiscate land, and distribute it to poor peasants. Their words were contradictory, obviously intending to destroy China's economic and political organization. The "Where is China Going?" (Evidence No. 26), "This is the Broad Road of the Anti-Japanese and National Salvation Movement" (Evidence No. 26), "The Situation After the Second Resolution of the League of Nations" (Evidence No. 26), and "Appeal to Workers in Commemoration of May Day" (Evidence No. 26) published in his personal name, even regarded the Three Principles of the People as reactionary and advocated a third revolution, resolutely sweeping away the Kuomintang government and replacing the Kuomintang regime with a revolutionary people's regime. His intention to endanger the Republic of China is obvious. However, upon investigation of the procedures followed by the Communist Party, which originally included stages such as organizing groups, propagating doctrines, armed uprisings, and establishing a Soviet regime, it is observed that the defendant's actions only involved the propagation of communism and had not yet reached the stage of an uprising. However, with the purpose of endangering the Republic of China, he assembled and organized groups, and used written materials to engage in treasonous propaganda, which is conclusively proven. He should be held responsible.

(2) Peng Shuzhi's Part: The defendant Peng Shuzhi, also known as Zhang Cinan, is from Baoqing, Hunan. He graduated from Baoqing Middle School. In the tenth year of the Republic of China (1921), he joined the Communist Party in Changsha. In the same year, he went to Moscow to study. In the thirteenth year of the Republic of China (1924), he returned to China and served as a mathematics teacher at Shanghai University and was in charge of editing the New Youth Monthly and Guide Weekly. Until the sixteenth year of the Republic of China (1927), when the Kuomintang purged the Communists and the Communist Party split, the defendant leaned towards the Trotsky faction. Due to differences in strategy, he was expelled from the party by the Cadre faction. In the second half of the eighteenth year of the Republic of China (1929), he joined Chen Duxiu in forming the Left Opposition faction of the Chinese Communist Party and was elected as a member of the Standing Committee of the Central Executive Committee. On October 15 of this year, using the pseudonym Zhang Cinan, he was holding a weekly meeting at Xie Shaoshan's house with Pu Yifan, Wang Wu, Wang Zhaoqun, and others when he was arrested on the spot. The defendant is a member of the Standing Committee of the Central Executive Committee of the CCP Opposition (hereinafter referred to as the CCP Standing Committee) and is one of the masterminds of the party. He should be fully responsible for the reactionary propaganda documents published in the name of the party and the activities he directed. The reasoning is the same as for Chen Duxiu. The reactionary documents he personally published, such as "The Japanese Imperialists' Forcible Occupation of the Three Northeastern Provinces and the Ruling Class's Kuomintang" (Evidence No. 26), "The Meaning of National Unity Against Foreign Aggression" (Evidence No. 26), "The Stalinists' Assessment of the Manchurian Incident and the Crisis of the Anti-Japanese Movement" (Evidence No. 26), "The Lessons of the Shanghai Incident and its Future" (Evidence No. 26), and "The Lessons of One Year of the Manchurian Incident and the Awareness That the People Should Have" (Evidence No. 26), upon reading their content, all promote communism and even slander the Kuomintang as a running dog of imperialism. After examining its purpose and strategies, it is determined that it aims to endanger the Republic of China. However, it has not yet reached the stage of an uprising. His acts of using written materials for treasonous propaganda and assembling and organizing groups should be held equally responsible with Chen Duxiu.

(3) Wang Wu's Part: The defendant Wang Wu, originally named Song Fengchun, joined the Communist Party in the fourteenth year of the Republic of China (1925) through the introduction of Zuo Jun and was in charge of propaganda work. Later, he disagreed with the Cadre faction and was expelled from the party. He then joined the Trotsky faction. In May of last year, using the pseudonym Liu Menggeng, he organized a Communist Party organ with Zheng Chaolin. The Songhu Garrison Command discovered this and, together with the police, arrested the defendant. The Shanghai Provisional Military Tribunal sentenced him to six years in prison and sent him to the Second Jiangsu Prison to serve his sentence. Later, the defendant contracted a disease in prison and was approved for medical parole on October 5 of this year. He did not repent and continued to carry out Communist Party work and was elected as an alternate member of the CCP Standing Committee. On October 15, he attended a Communist Party meeting with Peng Shuzhi and others and was arrested along with them when the detectives arrived. The defendant has clearly admitted to joining the Communist Party and being responsible for propaganda work. Although the defendant does not admit to being promoted to an alternate member of the CCP Standing Committee and attending Communist Party meetings after being released on medical parole, the accomplice Xie Shaoshan stated in the police station and the Second Branch of the Jiangsu High Court (hereinafter referred to as the Second Branch of the High Court) that there were five members of the Standing Committee, namely Chen Duxiu, Peng Shuzhi, Pu Yifan, Luo Shifan, and Song Fengchun. The last person had just been released from the Caohejing prison and this was his first time attending a meeting. I was arrested on the day we were holding our weekly meeting, etc. (pages 21 and 46 of the Second Branch of the High Court volume). Peng Shuzhi and Chen Duxiu also stated that the defendant was an alternate member of the Standing Committee (pages 51 and 52 of Volume 2 of this office), which is consistent with Xie Shaoshan's testimony. It is conclusively proven that the defendant attended the meeting and was elected as an alternate member of the CCP Standing Committee, and he cannot deny it. Moreover, while carrying out a crime, he committed the same crime again, and the circumstances are more serious. It is requested that he be severely punished.

(4) Pu Yifan's Part: The defendant Pu Yifan firmly denies joining the Communist Party and being elected as an alternate member of the Standing Committee. However, he was arrested while attending a weekly meeting at Xie Shaoshan's house, and reactionary books were found in his residence at No. 322 Gaofu Lane, Shengmuyuan Road. The accomplice Xie Shaoshan stated that the Standing Committee included five members: Chen Duxiu, Peng Shuzhi, Song Fengchun, and Pu Yifan (also known as Bu Deze), etc. (page 21 of the Second Branch of the High Court volume). When the judge of the Second Branch of the High Court asked what Peng Shuzhi's position was, she replied that he was a member of the Standing Committee. When asked about Pu Yifan and Wang Wu, she replied that they were also members of the Standing Committee (page 46 of the Second Branch of the High Court volume). Chen Duxiu stated in this office that there were three members of the Standing Committee. Besides me and Peng Shuzhi and Zhang Jiu, Pu Yifan and Song Fengchun were both alternate members of the Standing Committee (page 51 of Volume 2 of this office). The accomplice Peng Shuzhi, when asked in this office about Xie Shaoshan's statement that there were five members of the Standing Committee, replied that two were alternate members of the Standing Committee. When asked who the alternate members of the Standing Committee were, he said Song Fengchun and Pu Yifan (page 52 of Volume 2 of this office). Taking all of the above into consideration, it is highly credible that the defendant is an alternate member of the Standing Committee of the CCP Opposition. Moreover, the defendant was arrested on the spot while attending a meeting. If he were not a member of the Standing Committee, how could he participate? It is beyond doubt that the defendant joined a group assembled to endanger the Republic of China.

(5) Wang Ziping's Part: The defendant Wang Ziping, also known as Zeng Meng, is from Wenzhou, Zhejiang. In the twelfth or thirteenth year of the Republic of China, he went to Guangdong to apply for the Whampoa Military Academy but failed. Through a friend's introduction, he served as a clerk at the academy and then transferred to the Guangzhou General Labor Union, where he worked as a secretary. He resigned due to low pay and drifted around Guangzhou for several years. In the sixteenth year of the Republic of China (1927), through the introduction of his friend Qin Dingyu, he became a proofreader at the Chongwentang Printing House on Jiangwan Road in Shanghai. He joined the Communist Party at the persuasion of Hao Qianzhi, the deputy manager of Chongwentang. In October of the same year, he was sent to Moscow to study at Sun Yat-sen University. In the seventeenth year of the Republic of China, he returned to China due to illness and became involved with the Left Opposition faction. He was expelled from the party by the Cadre faction and joined the Trotsky faction. He was responsible for copying, printing, and distributing propaganda documents for the party. When he was arrested, the defendant was printing "School Life" and "Spark," claiming that the party instructed him to print 100 copies of "School Life" and 250 copies of "Spark." Given his actions, he joined a Communist Party organization and helped to spread communist propaganda. He has confessed to this without dispute and should be held criminally responsible.

(6) He Afang's Part: The defendant He Afang, also known as He Fang and He Zhi, is from Ruian, Zhejiang. In the fifteenth year of the Republic of China, he arrived in Shanghai. In February of the sixteenth year, he joined the Communist Party organization through the introduction of his friend Jin Muhun, also known as Jin Shisheng, and served as a messenger, receiving 25 yuan a month. In September of the sixteenth year, he was sent to the Eastern University and Sun Yat-sen University in Moscow to study communism for about three years. After graduating, he worked as a coppersmith in a red factory for about half a year and was expelled from the country. In April of the twentieth year of the Republic of China, he returned to Shanghai and worked as a coppersmith in factories such as Zhuoqun Machinery. He then joined the Trotsky faction. On September 23 of this year, he moved to the lower floor of No. 335 Yeguang Lane, Tangshan Road, and jointly printed reactionary publications, leaflets, and other documents of the CCP Opposition with Wang Ziping. All of the above facts have been stated in detail by the defendant in the police station, the Second Branch of the High Court, the Public Security Bureau, and this office. When he was arrested, he was engaged in printing work, and a large number of reactionary documents such as "Spark" and "School Life" were seized on the spot, which is consistent with his confession. The defendant joined the Communist Party organization and helped to spread communist propaganda. The evidence and testimonies are solid and conclusive and should be prosecuted according to the law.

(7) Wang Zhaoqun's Part: According to the defendant Wang Zhaoqun, he is from Suxian, Anhui. In October of this year, through the introduction of his friend Li Sichang, he was instructed to go to Shanghai to find Xie Shaoshan for work and stayed at Xie Shaoshan's home. He was arrested together with Peng Shuzhi and others on October 15 and firmly denies joining the Communist Party. Xie Shaoshan's home was the central organ of the Communist Party and was often used for meetings and discussions, which Xie Shaoshan has repeatedly stated clearly. Moreover, the Communist Party is a secret organization, and its meeting places are extremely strict. It does not allow outsiders to be present. Furthermore, he was arrested while a meeting was in progress. If the defendant did not have any qualifications, why would he be allowed to attend and participate? Since he was arrested on the spot, there is no doubt that he is a communist who joined a group and attended meetings.

(8) Guo Jinghao's Part: Guo Jinghao is Peng Shuzhi's younger brother and his original name was Peng Daozhi. There is a Communist Party school registration form to prove this (page 66 of Volume 2 of this office). According to the registration form, the defendant is currently 23 years old. In September of the fourteenth year of the Republic of China (1925), he joined the Communist Party in Changsha, Hunan. He later withdrew from the relationship in an informal way. In December of the eighteenth year of the Republic of China (1929), he joined the Opposition in Shanghai. He had previously engaged in student movements. After joining the Opposition, he was engaged in the district committee and student movements in the eastern district of Shanghai and is currently responsible for organizational committee work and student movements. According to this record, the defendant is highly suspected of joining a Communist Party organization.

(9) Liang Youguang's Part: On October 15 of this year, after the Communist Party's central organ in Chunyang Lane, Dongyouheng Road, was cracked down, several scraps of paper with communication addresses were seized. Based on these addresses, the detectives went to ambush No. 1044 Siwen Lane, Datong Road. Because it was late at night, the defendant and others were nervous due to their guilt. Another person escaped by jumping out of the window, but the defendant Liang Youguang was chased and captured after jumping out of the window and running for more than ten steps (page 44 of the Second Branch of the High Court volume). Various reactionary books were seized in the house. When questioned, the defendant firmly claimed that the reactionary books did not belong to him. However, since the defendant is not a member of the Communist Party, he should have sat quietly in the room and waited for the search. Why would he be so panicked? The Shanghai Public Security Bureau has verified that the defendant is an inspector of the CCP Opposition in various provinces and had just arrived in Shanghai from Guangxi. There is an official letter from the Shanghai Public Security Bureau to prove this (page 64 of Volume 2 of this office). There is considerable evidence that the defendant is a member of the Communist Party. His claim that he was looking for his younger brother Liang Youming is obviously an excuse and cannot be believed.

(10) Wang Jiantang's Part: The defendant Wang Jiantang repeatedly denied participating in Communist Party work when questioned. After reviewing the files of the Second Branch of the High Court, it was found that the detectives went to arrest him based on the communication address scraps seized at Xie Shaoshan's house, and also seized ten types of reactionary books at the defendant's home. The defendant claimed that the books belonged to Wang Boping, a resident on the upper floor. However, Wang Boping could not be found and summoned, and the defendant's name matched the name of the communication seized at the central organ of the Communist Party. There is a report from Western Detective Gode of the police station that can be cited as evidence (page 45 of the Second Branch of the High Court volume). It is clear that the defendant is a member of the Communist Party.

In conclusion, Chen Duxiu, Peng Shuzhi (Zhang Cinan), Pu Yifan, Wang Wu (Song Fengchun), Wang Yuping, He Afang, Wang Zhaoqun, Guo Jinghao (Peng Daozhi), Liang Youguang, and Wang Jiantang organized groups or assemblies for the purpose of endangering the Republic of China and have violated Article 6 of the Emergency Law on Punishing Crimes Endangering the Republic of China. Moreover, Chen Duxiu and Peng Shuzhi used written materials to engage in treasonous propaganda, and Wang Ziping and He Afang helped with treasonous propaganda, which is highly suspected of violating Article 2, Paragraph 2 of the same law. The seized communist books and documents were used for committing crimes and preparing for crimes and should be confiscated in accordance with Article 10 of the same law and Article 60, Paragraphs 1 and 2 of the Criminal Law. A public prosecution is hereby filed in accordance with Article 253, Paragraph 1 of the Criminal Procedure Law.

Appeal of Songxing Bank Creditors 85

Requesting the County Court to Correct the Original Ruling

Impartial Judgment Requested Against Defendants Who Have Not Withdrawn

Regarding the Songjiang Bank debt case, the County Court sent out the original ruling on the 26th. Bai Guanlan and others applied for an appeal on the 27th. Yesterday (the 29th), they listed legal provisions to supplement the grounds for the appeal as follows: "㈠ Article 53 of the Code of Civil Procedure concerns necessary joint litigation. This case is not a necessary joint litigation, but an ordinary joint litigation. Since it is an ordinary joint litigation, Article 52 of the same law naturally applies. This is self-evident. ㈡ Why is this case not a necessary joint litigation? Necessary joint litigation has an inseparable nature from the beginning. The rationale of the same law takes easements as an example. Shi Zhiquan's annotated explanation of the Civil Procedure Regulations further cites the revocation of betrothals as examples. This kind of litigation objective with unified determination is fundamentally indivisible. It is very different from the joint defendants of joint and several debts, because suing one person or a part of the joint and several debtors is also effective. In other words, it is divisible everywhere. ㈢ Whether or not a debt is unified and determined is originally stipulated in substantive law. Article 272, Paragraph 2 of the Civil Code stipulates that the establishment of joint and several liability is limited to cases where the law provides for it. Article 681 of the same law states that when the partnership property is insufficient to pay off the debts of the partnership, each partner shall be jointly and severally liable for the deficiency. Since Songjiang Bank has not been legally registered as a company, it cannot be regarded as a legal person and a partnership. Since it is a partnership, the creditor can naturally request full or partial payment from one or several or all of the debtors simultaneously or sequentially (see Article 273 of the Civil Code). Its nature is not only simply divisible, but also the creditor has the right to choose whether to divide or not, and there is absolutely no opposing provision. Since substantive law stipulates this way, procedural law naturally applies the articles for non-unified determination, namely Article 52 of the Code of Civil Procedure rather than Article 53. The original ruling stated that it is necessary to maintain the same state in substance, which means that the legal meaning of Article 273 of the Civil Code has not been considered. ㈣ It is found that Zhu Hezun and Gu Jiaxuan are part of the defendants. Withdrawing the case against these two is regarded as not suing these two. Moreover, when the withdrawal against the two was requested in court, the presiding judge asked why the withdrawal was made. The agent replied that it was because the two argued that they did not participate. Judge Pan then ordered the lawyer of the defendants Zhang Xiaolin etc. to argue. Then the lawyers of both parties debated each other. If the entire case was withdrawn, what would be the point of the debate? It is evident that the court did not consider the entire case withdrawn at that time. ㈤ Based on the above, the original ruling's citation of Article 53 of the Code of Civil Procedure is indeed erroneous, then the litigation costs cannot be applied according to Article 85 of the same law, but should

allow the substantive rights of the litigation to be decided in accordance with Article 87 of the same law. In short, the creditor's rights in this case are legally established, and the defendants should bear joint and several liability. The original ruling and your court's decision not to prosecute Zhang Xiaolin, etc. criminally has been explained in detail in the first half. The appellants are eager to appeal in accordance with the provisions of Article 449 of the Code of Civil Procedure, and request your court to review and verify and promptly correct the original ruling in accordance with the provisions of the first half of Article 457 of the same law, and to make a fair judgment on the joint defendants who have not withdrawn the case based on the prior complaint, and order the defendants to bear the litigation costs, for the sake of both public and private virtue."

Kidnapping Case Occurs in the Suburbs of Songjiang 86

In recent days, robbery cases have occurred frequently in Songjiang. Unexpectedly, the Wang Guoqing family in Shanjiaqiao, outside the East Gate, three miles from the city, was also kidnapped by bandits on the night of the 29th. The Wang family is well-off and has long been coveted by bandits. That night, a bandit boat was parked in the river behind the Wang residence. There were about twelve or thirteen bandits, each holding a pistol, who rushed into the Wang residence and looted it. Because they did not gain much, they were not satisfied with their desires, and forced Wang Guoqing to hand over 2,000 yuan. Wang said he had no means to produce it, and was immediately tied up and taken to the boat. Wang's grandmother, unable to bear her beloved grandson being taken away, immediately collected 300 yuan in cash and chased after the bandit boat, intending to redeem her grandson. However, the bandits took the money and still refused to release him. Helplessly, she reported to the County Public Security Bureau for arrest on the morning of the 30th.

Wuxi Rice Prices Gradually Decline 87

This year's rice prices have reached their lowest point. At the end of the year, sales are increasingly sluggish. However, the amount of goods arriving is not very large, so market prices are only slightly decreasing day by day. The reason for this is that it is the end of the year, and most merchants are preparing to close their books. Merchants from Jinan, Tianjin, and other regions come to Wuxi to purchase goods, but shipping takes time, and it is too late to transport them back within the year, so they have stopped buying. Judging from the situation, the rice market will not improve much within the year. Yesterday's market price dropped slightly by a few cents. Top-grade coarse japonica rice was six yuan and eight cents, down to six yuan and one cent. Coarse large-grain indica rice was six yuan and four or five cents, down to six yuan. Coarse sheep indica rice was six yuan and six or seven cents, down to six yuan and two or three cents. Coarse wharf indica rice was six yuan and four or five cents, down to six yuan. Coarse Hakka indica rice was five yuan and five or six cents to five yuan and one or two cents. Coarse Yuan rice was seven yuan and two or three cents to seven yuan. High-grade white japonica rice was seven yuan and one or two cents to six yuan and seven or eight cents, down to six yuan and five or six cents. White Yuan rice was eight yuan and two or three cents to eight yuan. White sheep indica rice was seven yuan to six yuan and seven or eight cents. White large-grain indica rice was six yuan and eight or nine cents to six yuan and five or six cents. White wharf indica rice was six yuan and eight or nine cents to six yuan and six or seven cents. Hakka white indica rice was six yuan and four or five cents to six yuan and one cent. Japonica rice was three yuan and nine cents to three yuan and seven cents. Sheep indica rice was three yuan and five or six cents to three yuan and two or three cents. Wharf indica rice was three yuan and four or five cents. Hakka indica rice was three yuan and three or four cents to three yuan and one cent. Yuan rice was four yuan and two or three cents to four yuan and one cent.

Chinese League for Civil Rights Holds Reception for Chinese and Foreign Journalists Yesterday 91

The Chinese League for Civil Rights held a reception for Chinese and foreign journalists at Hu'an Building at 4:00 pm yesterday. More than 30 journalists from local newspapers, magazines, and news agencies attended. Madam Sun Yat-sen, Ms. Soong Ching Ling, the chairman, was absent due to a cold. The reception was hosted by the vice-chairman Cai Yuanpei and the general secretary Yang Xingfo, who reported on the purpose of the organization and the current situation of the League for Civil Rights. After the report, Chinese and foreign journalists stood up one after another to express their opinions on the freedom of speech and publication. Vice-Chairman Cai Yuanpei gave satisfactory answers. The guests and hosts enjoyed themselves until about 6:00 pm. Details of the event are described below.

Madam Sun's Speech 92

Yesterday, Madam Sun was absent due to illness and sent a letter to express her apologies. After the journalists were all present, Chairman Cai Yuanpei stood up and read her speech on her behalf. It said, in brief, "Today is the day when the Chinese League for Civil Rights is hosting the Shanghai press. On behalf of the League, Qingling extends sincere wishes and welcomes to all of you. The press and the members of the League for Civil Rights share the responsibility of promoting the progress of human society. Therefore, I believe that, in theory, we should have a united front and faithful cooperation for our common mission. The purpose of the League is to assist all struggles for the freedom of association, assembly, speech, and publication. In other words, the League for Civil Rights is a fighter and defender of freedom of publication. Therefore, from the perspective of the publishing industry itself, it seems that this League should be given sincere support. One important point that Qingling would like to solemnly present to you is that the League's greatest effort is to assist the vast majority of political prisoners who are in prison without help or knowledge. As members of the press, you are well aware of the illegal detention of many of our countrymen and the existence of secret military trials, a relic of the Middle Ages. Will you remain silent and not protest against these things, or will you work together with the League for Civil Rights to shoulder this mutual responsibility?"

Cai Yuanpei's Speech 93

Today, the founders of the League and I are hosting the journalists of this city. I am extremely grateful for your presence and guidance. Madam Sun has explained the intention of the League and its close relationship with the press. I would like to share my personal thoughts. What we want to protect is human rights, and our object is human beings. Since we are all human beings, we have a common and universal human right that should be protected. Therefore, first, we have no partisan prejudice, because what each party is fighting for has gone beyond universal human rights. We will never work exclusively for one party and disregard others. Second, we have no national boundaries, because whether someone is from country A or country B, since we are all human beings, we should not discriminate based on nationality. However, there is a difference in the opportunity to serve people depending on whether the location is near or far. We have more opportunities to serve people in our own country and fewer opportunities to serve foreigners. But foreigners also have their own comrades who can easily serve them. According to the division of labor, there is no difference. Third, we do not discriminate between those who have been convicted and those who have not. It is a matter of course that the human rights of those who have not been convicted should not be trampled on. For those who have been convicted, if they are innocent, there is of course a need for relief. As for those who have been convicted and are not innocent, if we follow the psychology of hating evil as an enemy, it seems that we can ignore everything. However, criminologists attribute human sins to physiological defects, and socialists attribute them to social causes. Even at the root of punishment befitting the crime, there is still room for consideration. Therefore, the ancients had the admonition "If you know the circumstances, have pity and do not rejoice," and the observation of tracing the past and understanding the truth. Even under legal sanctions, we must recognize that punishment befitting the crime is natural and should not be added to beyond the natural punishment. If there is any addition, there is also a need for protection, such as private torture and abuse in prisons. Therefore, we do not discriminate against those who are innocent or guilty. The news you preside over may be out of patriotism and give special care to your own country, or it may be because you have a special relationship with one party and often have the attitude of supporting party A and attacking party B in political views. This is indeed inevitable and unavoidable. However, I hope that you can transcend national and party relations in protecting universal human rights and make judgments accordingly. This is what I hope for.

Yang Xingfo's Report 94

Then, the general secretary of the association, Yang Xingfo, reported that the League was founded only half a month ago and has only established a temporary executive committee to handle the work. The purpose is to fully protect civil rights. In the future, branches will be established in Beijing, Shanghai, and Pingjin. Li Jizhi has been entrusted to handle the work in Beijing. Nanjing is being entrusted to handle the work. Because Shanghai has not yet publicly solicited members, the branch has not been formally organized and established. The formal executive committee must be established after the branches are established, and then the executive committees from various places will be convened to hold a national executive committee meeting, from which the formal executive committee will be produced. Today, we are hosting all the journalists, ㈠ hoping that you can understand the organization of our association, ㈡ hoping that all of you present will take the lead in joining our association, etc.

Telegram to the Pingjin Authorities 95

The League's Provisional Executive Committee has been established, with Soong Ching Ling as Chairman, Cai Yuanpei as Vice-Chairman, Yang Xingfo as General Secretary, and Lin Yutang as Director of Publicity. Dr. Li Jizhi gave a speech in Shanghai the other day, expressing his sympathy for the League's purpose of helping young people, and especially considering inspecting prisons in the interior and acting as a voluntary duty. The Executive Committee entrusted Dr. Li to be responsible for organizing a branch in Beiping after arriving in Beiping. In addition, the association sent another telegram to the Beiping Public Security Bureau regarding the recent illegal detention of dozens of teachers and students in Beiping, hearing that only Xu Deheng was released on bail by President Jiang of Peking University. The telegram reads as follows: "Bao, Director of the Beiping Public Security Bureau, Greetings. We have heard that only Xu Deheng has been released on bail among the teachers and students illegally detained in Beiping, and the remaining dozens are still detained by your bureau. The government is strongly advocating the protection of all freedoms of the people, but how can your bureau explain its actions? We urge you to release all the detained teachers and students immediately in order to respect public opinion and protect civil rights. We look forward to a reply by telegram. Soong Ching Ling and Cai Yuanpei, Chairman and Vice-Chairman of the Chinese League for Civil Rights."

The payment will be made by the five banks of Central, China, Communications, National Products, Jiangsu, and Zhejiang, starting on the 31st of this month.

Issuance Process 104

Yesterday, the reporter of New Sound News interviewed Qin Runqing, the chairman of the fund management committee, who talked about the issuance process: (A) Regarding the issuance of bonds, ㈠ the total amount is 3 million yuan, of which 1,000 tickets are for 1,000 yuan each, totaling 1 million yuan, and 20,000 tickets are for 100 yuan each, totaling 2 million yuan. ㈡ Starting from December 26th, the China National Products Bank is entrusted to issue the bonds on the basis of the subsidy vouchers issued by the Committee for the Sorting of Chen Factory Silk and Chen Jian. (B) Regarding the bond fund, ㈠ the first principal and interest of 232,500 silver yuan was allocated to the fund on December 24th and deposited into the China National Products Bank, and then allocated to the banks that pay the principal and interest. ㈡ According to the regulations, the bonds will be issued from October 1st of the 21st year until December 31st of this year. The first installment of interest should be paid, so the first installment of interest will be paid while the bonds are being issued. (C) Regarding the bond lottery, ㈠ the total amount of this bond is 3 million yuan, with a term of 16 months. The principal will be redeemed every three months. Each time, 187,500 silver yuan should be redeemed, but because the odd amounts below 10,000 yuan are not enough for one lottery ticket, it is stipulated that six tickets will be drawn for each of the first, second, and third lotteries, and seven tickets will be drawn for the fourth lottery. For the following 13 lotteries, six tickets will be drawn three times, and seven tickets will be drawn once, so 100 tickets will be drawn by the end of the 16th period. ㈡ The personnel who execute the lottery affairs will be assigned by the Central, China Communications, Jiangsu, and Zhejiang banks, each sending one person to be responsible, according to the lottery procedure.

Central Mint to Begin Casting on March 1, Year 22 107

Yesterday, a reporter met with Finance Minister Song and had the following conversation. According to Minister Song, the Shanghai Central Mint plans to begin casting on March 1, Year 22. For those entrusting silver for casting, each yuan will cost approximately seven mace, one candareen, and five cash of silver. Furthermore, the Central Mint can create silver bars with a purity of 999/1000, and the pure silver content will be equivalent to 1,000 new silver coins. The Mint will also charge a casting fee for those requesting the Mint to cast silver bars. The calculation of the casting fee will be equivalent to the casting fee for 1,000 new silver coins, plus the refining fee. The amount of the refining fee will depend on the type of silver submitted. Minister Song also stated that a Shanghai Central Mint Advisory Committee will be formed, comprised of leaders from the financial, industrial, and commercial sectors, to assist the Mint in maintaining the legal purity of the new silver coins. In addition, renowned chemical testing experts will be hired as chemists for the Mint. Minister Song's plan, if realized, will likely prevent the Shanghai tael exchange rate from being higher than the current market rate.

Public Concession Increases Number of Chinese Land Commissioners 108

Selection Procedures Still Under Dispute: In early summer of this year, the Chinese Ratepayers' Association of the Public Concession passed a resolution to increase the number of Chinese Land Commissioners by two. They directly negotiated with the Concession authorities to implement this. Subsequently, the Consul General of the Protecting Power in Shanghai agreed. However, according to Article 28 of the Yangjingbang Regulations, the local officials' consent is required. Therefore, British Consul General Brenan and American Consul General Cunningham addressed Mayor Wu in late July. However, the Municipal Council believes that the nominees should be subject to the Council's approval. Thus, in early October, the Chinese Ratepayers' Association directly sent a letter to the Municipal Government, expressing their opposition to the Council's approval, and requested that negotiations be conducted with Consul General Cunningham, the leader of the consular body. In mid-October, the Municipal Government forwarded the Chinese Ratepayers' Association's opinion to Consul General Cunningham for review. It is now known that Mr. Cunningham replied a few days ago, which has been sent to the Municipal Government, and the Municipal Government has forwarded it to the Ratepayers' Association for review. The original letter from the Municipal Government to the Chinese Ratepayers' Association is transcribed below:

Respectfully, the following is an excerpt from the letter from the American Consul General and Leader of the Consular Body: Regarding the addition of two Chinese commissioners to the Land Commission, the Leader of the Consular Body forwarded a proposal to the Municipal Council on July 27, and approved the public letter of October 13. The Chinese Ratepayers' Association's public letter expressed opposition to the requirement that the two Chinese commissioner nominees in the proposal must be agreed upon by the Municipal Council and the Chinese Ratepayers' Association, and the Municipal Council and the Chinese Property Owners' Association. The opinions stated by the Association are very pertinent and reasonable. Based on this, the Council was asked to consider these opinions. Now, the Director-General of the Council has replied, stating that after further consideration, the Council believes that if Item A of the resolution passed by the Western Ratepayers' Annual Meeting is retained, it can be implemented accordingly. Item A was contained in the letter of July 27, namely, "A. One of the two newly added Chinese Commissioners to the Land Commission must be appointed by the Chinese Ratepayers' Association. The appointee must not be a property owner or a representative of a property owner. The other commissioner shall be appointed by the Chinese Property Owners' Association." As such, if the Chinese Commissioners are appointed separately by the Ratepayers' Association and the Property Owners' Association according to the above method, the Municipal Council is willing to withdraw the restriction stated in Item B of the previous letter that the approval of the Municipal Council is required. However, as stated in the Ratepayers' Association's public letter of October 13, the Ratepayers' Association and the Property Owners' Association must still exchange opinions with the Chinese directors of the Municipal Council when selecting the Chinese Commissioners. Now that the Municipal Council has responded to the Chinese Ratepayers' Association's wishes regarding the selection of Chinese Commissioners, it is hoped that Your Honorable Mayor will provide written confirmation of agreement to the Municipal Council's revised proposal. If it is necessary to amend the Yangjingbang Regulations, we can submit our opinions to the Diplomatic Body. A response is requested. Respectfully, etc. Based on this, the previous letter was duly forwarded for your information. Now, in accordance with the preceding, a corresponding letter is sent for your review, and a prompt response is requested. Respectfully, Shanghai Public Concession Chinese Ratepayers' Association, Wu Tiecheng, Mayor of Shanghai.

Japanese Naval Activities in China 109

Large-Scale Naval and Land Exercises: Vice Admiral Minei, Commander of the Japanese Third Fleet, has summoned all of his warships to conduct exercises at Songkou on January 4, which is next Wednesday. At the same time, the flagship Izumo, the cruiser Tenryu, and 1,200 sailors will be assembled, together with 1,000 infantry and artillerymen from the Shanghai-based Special Naval Landing Force, to hold large-scale naval and land exercises. It is reported that the area from Hongkou to Jiangwan has been designated as the exercise location. The exercise subjects have been agreed upon by Minei and Sakano. The commander will be Major General Sakano of the Landing Force, and Minei will be the inspector of the large-scale exercises. The exercises will take place from 9:00 AM to 5:00 PM, during which time shooting and artillery fire will be involved. Military communications during the exercises will be relayed using the military telephone lines on North Sichuan Road.

Japanese Warships on the Yangtze River: The Japanese Navy on the Yangtze River attaches great importance to inspecting our country's fortifications and artillery positions and firing live ammunition. Japanese warships stationed along the upper and lower reaches of the Yangtze River have been assembled by Rear Admiral Sugisaka, Commander of the First Overseas Dispatch Force, after arriving in Hankou aboard the flagship Ataka. The ship captains will discuss various measures for guarding the Yangtze River.

More Police Arrive: The Japanese Consulate in Shanghai has increased its police force. During the months of September, October, and November, large groups of Japanese police, totaling as many as 200, have been dispatched, and have been divided into squads by Koketsu to carry out their duties. In December, another six or seven batches, totaling several dozen people, arrived to join the police force. Recently, a large number of Japanese police, including Morita, Ohara, Sato, Okamoto, Takeshi, Takahashi, Bunkichi, Yamakawa, Kitani, Suenaga Junji, and Fukushima, totaling more than 20, have been dispatched. The number of Japanese police in Shanghai is increasing.
