Overseas Chinese Deported from Japan 111

Hua Guoxi, a Chinese worker who was a barber in Japan, was deported back to Shanghai during the Shanghai war and resided on Wusong Road. In mid-December, he took the Japanese ship Mikasa Maru to Yokohama again. After purchasing a ticket and boarding the ship, he hurriedly misplaced his Japanese police permit. Fearing that he would not be able to disembark in Yokohama, Hua landed in Osaka. Hua secretly disembarked in Osaka, intending to avoid the scrutiny of the Japanese police in Yokohama, which led to his detention. Since Hua had friends in Osaka, he thought he could obtain a guarantee to avoid any unexpected incidents. However, after Hua disembarked, the Japanese police discovered him and telegraphed to various places to conduct a thorough search. Hua was greatly alarmed upon hearing this news and rushed from Osaka to Kyoto to take temporary refuge. However, the police were everywhere, and Hua was arrested as soon as he arrived in Kyoto. He was sent to the Osaka Police Station on the 26th of this month and imprisoned. The original plan was to put him on the Asosan Maru to Shanghai, but due to a lack of time, a telegram was sent yesterday to change the plan to the original ship, Mikasa Maru, which will arrive in Shanghai on January 2. At that time, he will be transferred to the Public Security Bureau to recover all expenses. Before this incident, a group of overseas Chinese, including Lin Shengyou, Lu Dehai, He Congzheng, and Yang Zhaofu, traveled from Shanghai to Japan and were detained by the Kobe Water Police Station. They were not allowed to disembark and were sent back to Shanghai on the original ship. Each person had prepaid in cash, which was deducted as travel expenses, so they suffered both mentally and financially.

Jin Changcheng Does Not Betray His Duty in the Face of Disaster 112

A Crew Member of the Ill-Fated New Fu Tai is a Model of Social Service: The New Fu Tai vessel struck a reef at Jigu Reef at 4:45 AM on the 26th of this month. The vessel immediately sent out a distress signal via wireless radio, which was received by the Shanghai Coast Radio Station, the China Merchants Steam Navigation Company Radio Station, and the Tongshun Steamer. The report was immediately made to the shipping company, and the Tongshun Steamer sailed to the vicinity of the distressed vessel, rescuing over twenty crew members by sampan. When the sampan went to rescue a second time, the New Fu Tai was gradually sinking, but the vessel's radio operator continued to communicate and call for help with the rescuers. The captain, seeing that the situation was critical, rushed to the radio room and urged the radio operator to quickly escape to the sampan. However, the radio operator, with a strong sense of responsibility, was unwilling to leave. The captain and the first mate, seeing that the situation was hopeless, forcibly pulled him out and lowered him into the sampan by a rope from the side of the ship. At that time, the wind and waves were very strong, and the sampan was swaying and unstable. With a single misstep, he was submerged. At first, he stretched out his arms and called for help, but a wave swept him away, and he disappeared in an instant. At the same time, the sampan capsized, and the captain, first mate, and over twenty other people were also in distress. The above is according to the eyewitness accounts of the rescued crew members. The wireless radio operator's name was Jin Changcheng, a native of Jiangning, Jiangsu, 21 years old, with an elderly father who depended on him for a living. He was a first-class graduate of the Shanghai China Wireless Radio Engineering School, excelling in both character and academics, and was highly valued by his teachers. He was especially responsible in his service, so he remained calm in the face of disaster and worked hard to call for help, ultimately enabling some of the crew members to be rescued. Mr. Jin sacrificed his life because of his strong sense of responsibility and his escape was the last. Mr. Jin is truly a model of social service.

Record of the Trial of Male and Female Members of the Blood Soul Anti-Traitor Group 115

The Group's Headquarters Were Located in the Unified Hotel; The Police Have Arrested Five Group Members; The Trial Was Held Yesterday; The Court Was Heavily Guarded; The Prosecutor Stated That It Meets the Requirements for Exemption from Prosecution

Following the arrest and conviction of Yun Huifang, a member of the Blood Soul Anti-Traitor Group, seven more people, including Liu Chongwu, were arrested. The police filed a lawsuit with the First Special Court. Details of the trial on the afternoon of the previous day were reported in yesterday's newspaper. Unexpectedly, on the 22nd of this month, five more men and women, including Luo Sizhang, were arrested and sent to the First Special Court for interrogation and detention. Since the police investigation was not yet complete, the court ordered a temporary postponement of the publication. The investigation has now been completed, and the trial was held publicly by the First Special Court yesterday morning. The detailed circumstances are recorded below:

The Arrest: Zhao Bingkun, the Chinese Deputy Inspector of the General Inspectorate of the Public Concession Police, after detaining Yun Huifang and Liu Chongwu, members of the Blood Soul Anti-Traitor Group whose sole purpose was to eliminate traitors, secretly investigated the group's headquarters and accomplices. It was not until the 22nd of this month that the room number 41 in the Unified Hotel on Beihai Road, which was the group's headquarters, was discovered. At 2:00 PM, he led the Fourth District detectives to raid the room. In the room, four people were arrested: Luo Sizhang (also known as Luo Yixin), 20 years old, from Anhui; Lu Yong, 16 years old, from Pudong; Wu Hongsheng, 18 years old, from Shanghai; and Zhang Guifang, 18 years old, a woman from Pudong. A large amount of explosives, two bombs, and raw materials for making bombs were confiscated and taken back to the police station. Under questioning, it was learned that there were other accomplices hiding in the Yongyu Qianzhuang on Ningbo Road. Subsequently, Hong Zhifang, 20 years old, from Shaoxing, was arrested. In Hong's home at No. 105 Haig Road, an empty bomb shell, a bomb design, and six rifle bullets were confiscated and brought back to the police station, where they were detained separately. They were then sent to the First Special Court. Because the crime had not yet been clarified, the police lawyer requested permission to detain them, which the court granted.

The Crimes: The police then began to investigate. The results showed that Luo Sizhang, Lu Yong, and Hong Zhifang obtained a hand grenade from Hong Zhifang at 5:00 PM on the 20th of this month and went with Luo Sizhang to throw the grenade at the Wanshun Chang Foreign Goods Store at No. 257 Nanjing Road, because they found that Wanshun Chang was selling Japanese goods. At that time, Luo stood at the intersection of Nanjing Road and Shanxi Road, while Lu went inside. Shortly after, he came out and threw the grenade inside. Unexpectedly, a fire broke out near Wanshun Chang at this time, and the fire brigade was doing its best to put out the fire, so Wanshun Chang was also watered, and the ground was full of water. Therefore, the grenade landed in the water and did not explode, and Wanshun Chang did not report the incident to the police. Therefore, the police did not know about it. After Luo and others confessed, the police took Luo and Lu to the store to demonstrate the situation at the time and asked the store if they had been bombed. The store denied being bombed but said that they had previously received warning letters from the Blood Soul Anti-Traitor Group Youth League. The police immediately ordered Luo et al. to make a list, detailing everything.

Court Security: Yesterday morning, the case was scheduled for trial. At 8:30 AM, the police escorted Luo et al. by car to the waiting room of the First Special Court Criminal Division. In order to prevent any unexpected incidents, a police car loaded with dozens of Chinese and Western police officers from the reserve team was dispatched to the gate of the court at Qipu Road. The car stopped in the middle of the road with a machine gun mounted on the roof for security. The Chinese Detective Chief Zhang Wenjun and the Western Detective Chief of the jurisdiction police station led the Chinese and Western police officers to the court to assist the bailiffs in maintaining order and preventing any disturbances. Personnel Present at the Hearing: At 9:10 AM, Qian Hongye, Chief Judge of the Criminal Division of the Special Court, Chief Prosecutor Wang Zuze, and Clerk Guan Zhiliang took their seats in the First Criminal Division. The police were represented by Lawyer Ru Baoyi, and the defendants were represented by Lawyers Yuan Yang'an, Qu Yue, and Xi Yafu. The police listed Luo Sizhang as the first defendant, Lu Yong as the second defendant, Wu Hongsheng as the third defendant, Zhang Guifang as the fourth defendant, and Hong Zhifang as the fifth defendant.

Prosecution Laws: Lawyer Ru Baoyi of the police first stated the articles of prosecution, saying that the police were prosecuting the five defendants for the crime of obstructing order by participating in a society whose purpose was to commit crimes, according to Article 161 of the Criminal Law, and for the crime of illegally possessing military firearms and explosives, according to Article 1 of the Regulations on the Prohibition of Military Firearms and Artillery. Since Luo, Lu, and Hong threw a bomb at Wanshun Chang, they were charged with the crime of obstructing freedom under Article 318 of the Criminal Law. Lawyer's Statement: When the defendants were arrested, a seal of the Blood Soul Anti-Traitor Group and a design for preparing to engrave the seal of the Zhongmin Patriotic Advancement Team were found, indicating that they were organized. A notebook was also confiscated, which contained records of their meetings, as well as the Zhongmin Patriotic Advancement Team's articles of association and declarations. Articles 7 and 8 of the articles of association state the methods of warning treacherous merchants, such as shooting, striking, or bombing. If anyone obstructs the progress, they will be dealt with by force. This shows that their organization is for the purpose of committing crimes, and the articles of association and declarations all bear the signatures of defendants one, two, three, and five. Although the fourth defendant is not named, she is also an accomplice and should be held responsible under Article 161 of the Criminal Law. The crime of illegally possessing explosives is also very clear, as dangerous goods were found in the defendants' places of arrest, so no explanation is needed. The crime of obstructing freedom committed by the defendants is also very clear. Because the defendants learned that Wanshun Chang was selling Japanese goods, they went to throw a bomb on the 20th of this month. Fortunately, it did not explode. The defendants also admitted that they had previously sent a warning letter, but the letter had been discarded by Wanshun Chang, so it is impossible to know what was said in it. The reports and confessions of each person were submitted to the court. The confessions of Luo and Hong were written in their own handwriting, while the rest were recorded by the police and signed and fingerprinted by the defendants.

Western Detective's Report: Western Detective Chief Gribble then testified that, "We first arrested the first, second, and third defendants in the Unified Hotel. Later, fearing that there were more revolutionaries, we sent detectives to guard the inside. At 10:30 AM, Zhang Guifang came, and the detective arrested her. Explosives were found on her. According to her, Luo Sizhang feared that these items would be dangerous in the inn, so he asked her to take them to her home. Because they were needed today, she was ordered to bring them back. Finally, Hong Zhifang was also arrested. Their group's first regular meeting was held on September 18 at No. 22 Guling Road, where it was decided to change the Blood Soul Anti-Traitor Group to the Zhongmin Patriotic Advancement Team. Luo Sizhang proposed to find a way to obtain small arms, and Wu Zhengming proposed to use hydrochloric acid and other things to warn treacherous merchants. The second regular meeting was held on November 24 at No. 9 Nanlin Lane, Haining Road. Cai Yaozu reported on the economic situation, Luo Sizhang reported on the preparations for weapons, and leaflets warning treacherous merchants and a warning letter to the Nanshi National Goods Market were passed. The contents of the leaflets were not only unfavorable to treacherous merchants, but also unfavorable to the police lawyer. At that time, we found a jar of road salt, which, according to Luo, belonged to Wang Shao-cheng of No. 209 Xizang Road. Wang is wanted by the police for the murder of Wang Zhengtao at No. 310 and No. 312 Xinzha Road. The bomb we seized was prepared to be sent to the Nanshi National Goods Market. The Wanshun Chang case was discussed and decided in advance at a meeting in Baik Road. Later, Detective Zhao and I led the second defendant, Luo, to the store to demonstrate the situation." Wang Shengmu, the assistant manager of Wanshun Chang, testified that "Our store does not sell enemy goods. However, the old inventory in the store must be sold due to capital constraints." He denied that a bomb had been thrown.

Defendant's Testimony: Defendant Luo Sizhang testified, "Although I am the Deputy Captain, I was actually used as a scapegoat by the group. All affairs were presided over by Cai Yaozu. I deny participating in the bombing of Wanshun Chang. I confessed because I was afraid of police torture. The truth is that on the 19th, Lu Yong told me that he was going to bomb Wanshun Chang. I dissuaded him. Unexpectedly, Lu came the next day and said that he had bombed the store. I severely reprimanded him, so I did not actually participate in this matter." The court then asked about the discussions with Zhang Guifang and the relationship between them. Luo replied that they met at the Renji Hospital and had no relationship. He was asked if it was because he was afraid that the explosives in the hotel would be dangerous that he ordered Zhang to take them for safekeeping. Luo replied that the item was given to him by Cai Yaozu and he did not know what it was. Later, Zhang came to his place to take it away. He did not know at first, but later, after Zhang took it away, he told her that it was dangerous and ordered her to send it back. He did not order her to take it away. He was asked whether Zhang Guifang had previously been fined 20 yuan by the court for soliciting customers as a prostitute, and there was a fingerprint record to prove it. He was asked whether he knew that she was a prostitute and had an affair with her, otherwise, why would he give her such an important item to take back and forth. He replied that there was no such thing. Zhang Guifang testified, "My younger brother was sick, so I accompanied him to the Renji Hospital for treatment. That's when I met Luo, and we have no relationship. On the morning of the 21st, I went to Luo's hotel and took the dangerous item from the drawer. Later, Luo told me that it was dangerous and ordered me to send it back, so I sent it back and was arrested." The court asked her if she had previously been fined for prostitution, and Zhang firmly denied it. Lu Yong testified, "Although I am a member of the Blood Soul Anti-Traitor Group, I did not throw the bomb. I confessed to the Wanshun Chang case because I was afraid of torture. I only know that Chen Guangxiang sent a warning letter to the store." The court asked if he had persuaded Wu Hongsheng to join the Blood Soul Group. He replied that he had not. Wu Hongsheng testified that he was friends with Luo Sizhang et al. and was a colleague in the Volunteer Army. Lu Yong did not persuade him to join the Blood Soul Group. Hong Zhifang was in the construction industry. Regarding the police's confession, he said that the detectives had written the draft and ordered him to copy it. He denied participating in the bombing. Start of Debate: At this point, the court ordered the start of the debate. Lawyer Ru Baoyi of the police stated that the defendants' organization of a group for the purpose of committing crimes and their bombing and intimidation were very obvious. According to their crimes, there was no excuse. However, the defendants were all very young, and this point could be forgiven. If the court gave a reduced sentence, his lawyer would agree and requested that a judgment be made according to the law. The defendants' representatives, Lawyers Yuan, Qu, and Xi, successively argued, generally dividing the following points: (1) Since the treacherous merchants are called treacherous and harm the interests of the Republic of China, the defendants' removal of them is not a crime. (2) The police cannot prove that the explosives were definitely possessed by the defendants. (3) The confession cannot be proven to be true. (4) The police lawyer's final conclusion is quite appropriate and should be given special attention. (5) Please refer to Articles 66 and 76 of the Criminal Law to grant a special reduced sentence and request that a suspended sentence be pronounced at the same time as the guilty verdict in accordance with Article 90 of the Criminal Law. Finally, Prosecutor Wang rose to state his opinion, saying that although the two articles of prosecution by the police can be divided into three situations, they are actually one act. According to Article 74 of the Criminal Law, a heavier sentence should be imposed. Since the defendants were motivated by patriotism, they violated the law. Considering their circumstances, they meet the requirements for exemption from prosecution. Please judge them according to the law. Scheduled Sentencing: Judge Qian then concluded the debate on the case and scheduled the sentencing for the morning of January 5. Wu Hongsheng and Zhang Guifang were allowed to post a 500 yuan bail bond each. The rest were detained. After the verdict was announced, the police security was also withdrawn at the same time. It was already past noon.

Another Ningbo-Style Sandboat 116

A Bold Undertaking to Circumnavigate the World Departing from Shanghai Next Month: According to the North China Daily News, a New Yorker named White Bromsheld has purchased a Chinese-style sandboat, only 65 feet long, and is modifying it. He named it New Horizon and plans to depart from Shanghai in January to circumnavigate the world. The ship was built in Ningbo and was completed just a year ago. It has already been sailing at sea for five months. When it departs in the future, in addition to White Bromsheld and Evansworth, four crew members will be hired. Initially, Chinese crew members will be hired, and in the future, it is hoped that Europeans will be used. The route will be from Shanghai to Hong Kong, then through the Philippines, Guam, Honolulu, through the Panama Canal, and then to Europe. Several months ago, a Chinese-style sandboat departed from Shanghai, and a Frenchman sailed it for a long ocean voyage, but unfortunately, it sank in Taiwan. This will be the second Chinese-style sandboat to circumnavigate the world.

Eight Ningbo Fishermen Rescued by the Shengjing Steamer 117

According to the North China Daily News, eight Ningbo fishermen recently drifted in the Yellow Sea and hoped to be rescued for twelve hours. They were rescued by the Taikoo Shingking Steamer on Wednesday morning and brought to Shanghai. The Ningbo Fellow-Provincials Association sent them back to their hometown. They left Shanghai on the Ningxing Steamer of the Sanbei Company yesterday (29th) afternoon. When they boarded the ship, they were so happy to have survived that they used the remaining money from the repatriation fee given by the Ningbo Fellow-Provincials Association to buy firecrackers and firecrackers, as well as peanuts and fruit, to share with the coolies and boat boys at the pier to celebrate. It can also be seen that their situation in the sea was dangerous and their rescue was unexpected, so they were extremely happy. It is said that eight people left Ningbo on a fishing boat several months ago. On Tuesday night in the Yellow Sea, they were suddenly hit by a steamer. The mast broke and the boat leaked, but the steamer broke through the waves and left as if nothing had happened. The eight people drifted on the sea, thinking that there was no hope of survival. Fortunately, the Shengjing Steamer, which was sailing from Tianjin to Shanghai, saw their mast sinking at about 9:00 AM on Wednesday morning. It rushed to the side of the ship, threw the cable to tie it up, and then pulled the eight people one by one onto the ship, giving them food and clothing. At that time, the boat was almost full of water and would sink in an instant. There was little hope that these people would not be buried in the belly of the fish. When the Shengjing arrived in Shanghai yesterday morning, the eight people were sent to the Water Patrol Police Station and transferred to the Ningbo Fellow-Provincials Association. It is now heard that the Customs authorities will be asked to thoroughly investigate the steamer that caused the disaster and did not provide assistance.

Zhou Fengyi's Bestial Acts 118

Accused of raping his eleven-year-old adopted daughter, the court should severely punish him. Shen Zhifa, a Ningbo native currently residing at 6 Annam Road in the French Concession, is 48 years old. He previously ran a coal business but became a vegetable vendor at a small market after losing his job. He has five daughters and two sons. Zhou Feng, a Tianjin native (37 years old), currently working as a needle worker but previously a constable residing at 17 Xicheng Lane, Ximen Road, in the French Concession, was an old neighbor. Zhou, after marrying, did not have children, so the couple was very fond of Shen's children. In July of last year, Shen's wife died, and he was burdened with the care of his children. Therefore, he gave his fifth daughter, Xiaomao (11 years old this year), to Zhou as an adopted daughter. At the time, Shen did not draw up a contract, nor did he receive any money from Zhou. Zhou took the girl to raise, and the two sides considered themselves relatives by adoption and visited each other from time to time. Unexpectedly, Zhou, a man with the face of a human but the heart of a beast, repeatedly raped the girl in the months of July, August, and November of this year and forbade her from speaking out. However, Xiaomao was young and not fully developed. After being violated, she fell ill, her face became yellow and emaciated, and her urethra was damaged, causing constant urination. Zhou did not provide medical treatment. Until the 27th of this month, for the 70th birthday of the girl's maternal grandmother, Shen went to Zhou's place and took Xiaomao to her grandmother's house to celebrate her birthday. In the afternoon, he wanted to send the girl back to Zhou's house, but the girl feared Zhou's abuse and refused to go back. Her grandmother thought the girl was being wilful and playful, so she kept her overnight and told Shen to pick her up the next day. The next day, the girl's grandmother wanted to send the girl back herself, but the girl cried and refused to go to Zhou's house again. When asked, she revealed the details of the rape. Her grandmother was shocked upon hearing this and immediately informed her son-in-law (the girl's father), who reported it to the French Concession police. Detective Zhu Junpei was dispatched to arrest Zhou. Meanwhile, the head detective ordered the girl to be sent to Guangci Hospital, where Doctor Brisset (professor of medicine at Aurora University) examined her and confirmed that the girl's hymen had been ruptured due to rape, issuing a diagnosis certificate to be attached to the case file by the police. Yesterday, the police escorted Zhou to the Second Special District Court, where Judge Xiong Huihua and Clerk Tao Zongkan presided over Criminal Court One to hear the case. The police lawyer, Gu Shouquan, explained the case, stating that the defendant had committed indecent acts against a minor and was being prosecuted under Article 243, Paragraph 1, Item 3 of the Criminal Code for offenses against public morals, requesting severe punishment according to the law. At this point, the court, considering the case to be one of public morals, inquired whether spectators should be prohibited. After questioning, the defendant directly confessed. The court ordered a date to be set for further interrogation and instructed the plaintiff, Shen Zhifa, to take the girl to the court's forensic doctor for examination in the afternoon for verification.

Reader's Advisory 122

(1) Why is education not doing well? Why is it that farmers don't have enough to eat?

[Letter from Mr. Gao Mianzhi]

I have two questions here. First, the education issue: Since I started working in rural education at the age of seventeen, it has been nine years. In the first five years, I was controlled by local bullies (school board members) and surrounded by petty people. Although I gained the trust of farmers, I resigned because I was from another place. In the summer of the eighteenth year, I admired the name of Xiaozhuang School and traveled to Ningbo with two or three like-minded comrades at our own expense to visit for more than a month. At the same time, the education sector of this county also organized a visiting group to go, but I have not heard any report from them about it. However, I, together with my comrades, went to four rural areas to find a school site and establish the school. For two years, there has been no assistance from the administrative authorities above, and jealousy from colleagues (education is not a profession) below, making progress extremely difficult! I now want to ask: (1) Why can't the local bullies who control education be overthrown? (2) Why are there no reports from those who went on official-funded visits? Why can't those who are interested in visiting get official funding? (3) Why do the administrative authorities verbally emphasize rural education but fail to provide actual assistance? (4) Why are colleagues jealous instead of cooperating? (5) Is working hard in rural education being a bookworm, and should people look at me as a bookworm? Second, the rural issue: In the rural society near the school, the people are diligent and thrifty, and they do not know about smoking or gambling. Last year, due to weather conditions, the rice harvest was not good. Even when it comes to firewood, this year's farmers are also feeling the pain of not having enough firewood to burn. Therefore, this year farmers have to eat rice that costs 16 yuan per dan; local products, in addition to rice, also include silkworm cocoons and beans and wheat in the spring and summer. Unexpectedly, this year's beans and wheat are almost so cheap that no one wants them, and silkworm cocoons are only one jiao per piece. This has already made the farmers suffer enough, but who knew there was some ×××; the army came to the countryside and stayed for more than two months. Although there were no major losses, the cost of providing for them was already very difficult! Alas! Unfortunate farmers, who could have imagined that they would have to suffer so much now? They worked hard for a year, and the rice matured, averaging five hu per mu, but who knew it was all in vain, and the rice price was only worth six yuan! Please look at their expenses: (1) Cattle fees (2) Rice fees (3) Grain tax (4) Mu tax (5) Rent rice (6) Account fees! Let's calculate the straw and rice fees: sixteen yuan plus interest requires three shi of rough rice to exchange for one shi of white rice! Therefore, there are several questions here that farmers asked me but I couldn't answer, so I am raising them all here and asking for answers: (1) Why is it that farmers don't have enough to eat? (2) Why are agricultural products such as rice, wheat, beans, and silk so cheap? (3) Why are things in stores so expensive? (4) Why are taxes so high? (5) What use do we have for the army?

...Reporter's note: The points raised by Mr. Gao are indeed very important issues at present. The reporter believes they are worthy of public discussion, so I am hereby inviting readers to discuss them together.

(2) What is it that everyone wants to say right now?

[Letter from Mr. Zhang Conglong]

My opinion: The Reader's Advisory section in Shen Bao is too boring. It is a very good and beneficial teacher, but it is just directing some lost people, and only providing some so-called unemployed people with some meaningless slogans, saying that the social environment is bad, or that they can't even find work, just waving their pens and complaining. You need to know that there are three conditions for finding work: First, you must ask yourself if you have the skills to work. Factories are not nursing homes, they don't want these amateurs. Second, can you endure hardship? Work requires effort. Third, then you can say that the society is bad and the government is incompetent. Why don't you open a few writing factories to support us? I don't believe that workers with skills and the ability to endure hardship will be unable to find food and starve to death. There are also some ladies, or disguised female geniuses, who open their mouths to say that marriage is bad, and ask for remedies, and close their mouths to say that the other party is bad, and seek free ways out, or create rumors and show off. I think in this world, not to mention that women are oppressed by their husbands, looking around, across the six continents, there is great oppression and small oppression, who is not living under oppression. I have never spoken empty words, but today I have caught the disease. As for communications discussing scientific knowledge, or texts seeking cooperation from all walks of life to start a business, then perhaps it can arouse the interest of some people.

Reply: After reading your letter, we feel that your thoughts are really contradictory. Since you know that everyone in the "world" is "living under oppression," why do you say that the "slogans" of "general" "unemployed people" are all "meaningless" "complaints"? Do you mean that many oppressed people should obey "oppression" to the end and should not have any resistance? The "badness" of the current society is known to anyone who usually pays a little attention to observing society, and you still say that this general cry is "complaining," then what kind of cry is considered "meaningful"? What is not "complaining"? We also know that working requires certain "skills" and the ability to "endure hardship," but is the current problem a problem of "skills" and "endurance"? Everyone can see how many people with "skills" and the ability to "endure hardship" are still inevitably "unemployed" and inevitably "starve to death." Whose fault is this? Are floods, droughts, wars, banditry, and all other "oppressions" "gifts" from "Old Man Heaven"? Or is it "bad human planning"? Are the crowds of unemployed people all unemployed because they lack "skills" and the inability to "endure hardship"? For example, if you want to start a "business" now, can your "skills" and ability to "endure hardship" alone make the business flourish? Are there other obstacles that will cause your business to fail in the end? Everyone is busy discussing reforms to address these serious problems in front of them, and you lightly dismiss them with the word "complaining," which really makes us "confused." As for the marriage issue, although many people have fought for it, even today, it is still not possible to universally obtain "freedom." The facts are also very clear, but you think that the purpose of the calls under this unfree oppression is to "show off." The immaturity of the theory is equally laughable. In short, we also know that we should now engage in so-called "construction" and should study more natural sciences. However, with society like this, unless there is a transformation first, how can we talk about anything? We have no preconceptions. We only know to follow everyone. What everyone says in their letters is what we will publish. You want us to publish more letters about studying "science" and "business," and we are not willing to do so, but what if the letters that come are all painful "slogans" and "complaints"?

Miscellaneous News 126

New Shanghai Esperanto Organization: Since the Shanghai Esperanto Association was destroyed in the Shanghai War, it has not been restored to this day. In view of this, enthusiastic Esperanto speakers in Shanghai held a Shanghai Esperanto Comrades' Get-Together on December 25th. More than 40 people attended, and all agreed that it was necessary to promote the Esperanto movement and organize an organization. A committee of nine people was elected to prepare for the establishment of the Shanghai Esperanto Speakers Association. The preparatory committee has already begun work, and once the preparations are complete, it will hold a general assembly in the near future to announce its establishment. It will widely solicit local and international Esperanto comrades and people from all walks of life who sympathize with Esperanto to join. It also plans to open Esperanto training classes during the winter vacation to meet the needs. It is reported that the preparatory committee is temporarily working at the China Correspondence School, No. 12, Dazhong Lane, Tongfu Road, and has begun processing membership registration procedures.

Scott Cup Football Tournament Semifinals

Jinan Sadly Eliminated 130

Two Players Injured Within the First Twenty-Five Minutes

Fighting with Only Nine Players Proves Too Difficult

"Lancashire Wins 3-2"

Yesterday, Jinan faced Lancashire in the Scott Cup semifinals at the Recreation Ground. Based on past performance, even without Chen Zhenhe and Luo Haiguang, Jinan should have been able to defeat Lancashire and secure a spot in the finals. Unexpectedly, fortune was not on their side, and misfortune struck repeatedly. Within the first twenty-five minutes, Jinan lost two major players, Xu Yahui and Zhong Guanming, due to injuries. Afterward, they had to play with only nine players. Despite their best efforts and scoring two goals, they were ultimately outnumbered and suffered a heartbreaking 3-2 defeat. Thus, Jinan was eliminated from the Scott Cup, leaving the blue-eyed, blonde-haired foreigners to compete for the championship. The lineups for both teams were as follows:

Lancashire:

Hill, Sarlefe, McDonald, Lyons, Ma Sheng, Zhao Bei, Lawton, Pitt, Barnes, Marius, Kai Zhi.

Jinan Team:

Liang Shutang, Liu Zukan, Gu Shang, Zhong Guanming, Xu Heng, Zhuang Shihong, Xu Yahui, Jiang Shanjing, Chen Zhenxiang, Xie Quanhe, Mei Hongbao.

Qiu Balian Scores Two Goals: What caught the eye in Jinan's lineup yesterday was Xie Quanhe, originally the goalkeeper, who was reassigned to right forward, with Xu Heng, famous in Hong Kong and Guangzhou, taking over as goalkeeper. However, Xu's skills did not stand out. As the match began, both sides were eager to win, and the competition was fierce. Jinan conceded a goal to Lancashire's center forward Lawton due to a misunderstanding between Jiang Shanjing and the goalkeeper, just five minutes into the game. At the same time, Zhong Guanming was injured and left the field. Amidst the chaotic struggle, Jinan launched several attacks, but none were effective. In the twentieth minute, Lancashire's Barnes scored again, making the score 2-0.

Jinan Returns the Favor: Having conceded two goals, Jinan was incensed and launched a full-scale counterattack. Less than five minutes later, Jiang Shanjing sent a long ball from the back, Mei Hongbao carried the ball forward, passing two defenders, and at a suitable spot, he passed it to Chen Zhenxiang, who seized the opportunity and scored, returning the favor. Amid the fierce battle, Zhuang Shihong was also suddenly injured, but fortunately, he recovered quickly. Unexpectedly, Xu Yahui was seriously injured and left the field in the twenty-fifth minute. After that, Jinan had to play with only nine players, greatly affecting their strength.

Liu Zukan Equalizes: After a brief break following the first half, Jinan showed great courage in one breath. Although there were only three forwards, each one was imposing and unmatched. Less than six minutes into the second half, winger Liu Zukan invaded the enemy territory, unstoppable, advancing to the corner and unleashing a powerful shot. The ball flew into the corner of the goal, a remarkable feat, with a very beautiful posture. Jinan thus tied the score at 2-2, escaping death and showing great potential for a comeback.

2-3 Agonizing Defeat: After tying the score at 2-2, Jinan's spirits were lifted. The three forwards were eager to try, constantly probing the enemy's stronghold. However, they lacked support and coordination, always feeling a lack of strength. Lancashire continued to attack fiercely, and Kai Zhi repeatedly displayed excellent skills. After about ten more minutes, Jinan's goal was suddenly surrounded, and they were attacked from all sides. Jiang Shanjing and Gu Shang worked tirelessly to defend, but Xu Heng was unable to cover everything. Thus, even the wisest man can make a mistake. In the long run, Lancashire's right inside forward Barnes scored, making the score 3-2. Afterward, Jinan's nine players rearranged their positions from time to time, hoping to make a desperate effort. However, they were outnumbered and lacked the strength, and they had no choice but to suffer a heartbreaking 3-2 defeat.

Hangzhou New Zhejiang Construction Games, Day One: Women's Basketball, Liangjiang Wins Over Southeast by One Point 133

Twenty-six to Twenty-five | Liangjiang Wins with Last Free Throw

Lin Baohua, Zheng Zhaojia, et al. | Tennis Exhibition Quite Outstanding

Today's Tennis Exhibition Continues | Today's Walking Race | Football Match

The Hangzhou New Zhejiang Construction Games invited Shanghai men's and women's teams to perform. Yesterday was the first day. In the afternoon, there was a tennis exhibition, with Lin Baohua, Zheng Zhaojia, and others participating. This morning, the tennis exhibition will continue. | The situation was consistently tense, with little to differentiate the teams.

| Liangjiang Gains Victory with the Final Free Throw

Final Score: Twenty-Six to Twenty-Five

The New Zhejiang Construction Games opened yesterday at the Hangzhou Provincial Stadium. The first match was a women's basketball exhibition, with Liangjiang winning against Southeast by one point with a score of twenty-six to twenty-five. In the last three minutes, both teams had scored twenty-five points each. In the final minute, Liangjiang's Yang Sen scored a free throw, which decided the victory. Southeast's Sun Yuxiu was also awarded a free throw before the end, but the ball missed the basket, resulting in a narrow one-point defeat, much to their regret. In terms of strength and performance, the two teams were evenly matched. The excitement and tension were rarely seen. The referee was Shu Hong.

Aircraft Show Before the match, students from the Central Aviation School in Qiaoli were asked to pilot two aircraft, soaring up and down around the stadium, sometimes high and sometimes low, either soaring straight into the clouds or plunging down, tumbling and performing various stunning maneuvers. Color leaflets were scattered temporarily, causing a scramble to grab them.

Hall Director Kicks Off It was not until 10:30 AM that Zeng Yangfu, the Director of the Construction Department, performed the opening kickoff ceremony. Approximately five to six hundred spectators were present. Director Zeng tossed the ball up, the referee blew the silver whistle, and Liangjiang and Southeast began competing for the ball. Hangzhou Mayor Zhao Zhiyou was also present to watch the game early.

Equal Situation Liangjiang and Southeast mutually attacked and defended, advancing and retreating, circling around. Yang Sen was found to have committed a technical foul. Sun Yuxiu tossed the ball up with both hands, and Southeast opened the scoring with one point. Pan Yueying scored two points with a mid-court long shot, and Southeast's momentum was strong, taking a three-point lead. Liangjiang repeatedly attacked, but Chen Rongming missed two opportunities to shoot under the basket. The ball went into the middle of the court, and Lu Xueqin and Zou Shande fought over the ball. Taking advantage of the situation, the ball rolled under the crotch, and Liangjiang's Chen Rongming intercepted it and went straight in. Lu Xueqin rushed to block it, but the ball went into the basket, and a foul was also called. Liangjiang scored three consecutive points, tying the score.

Liangjiang Takes the Lead Under this tied situation, Southeast continuously used long-range shooting tactics. Countless opportunities were missed, contrary to their wishes. In Pan's dream, Liangjiang exceeded the score by five to three. Pan Yueying tied the score again. However, Chen Rongming and Pan Meng scored again one after another. At the end of the first quarter, Liangjiang won by four points with a score of nine to five.

Amidst Tension After a two-minute break, Southeast fought hard and showed their skills. Pan Yueying and Wang Huizhen each scored a goal, immediately bringing the score back to nine to nine. Liangjiang's Chen Rongming added two more points, but Wang Huizhen did not show weakness, making it eleven to eleven, thirteen to thirteen. Seeing the tense situation, Liangjiang called another timeout, which was their third. Pan Yueying made a free throw, putting Southeast ahead of Liangjiang by one point, fourteen to thirteen. At the end of the first half, Yang Sen scored a goal amidst tight surveillance, putting Liangjiang ahead by one point with a score of fifteen to fourteen.

Tied Score After the lemon break, they decided the winner again. Yang Sen scored a free throw, but Pan Yueying's long shot made it sixteen to sixteen, eighteen to eighteen, twenty to twenty. During these eight minutes, it could be called the era of long-range shooting. It was difficult to develop further due to the excessively tight defense of both sides. The all-accurate shooting skills of both sides caused the entire stadium to marvel and lose color in comparison. At the end of the third quarter, Liangjiang was ahead by two points with a score of twenty-two to twenty.

Another Tie The final eight minutes of the deciding game were the most exciting part of the whole game. Chen Yingming scored three consecutive points, and Liangjiang suddenly took a commanding lead with a score of twenty-five to twenty, creating a winning momentum. However, Wang Huizhen suddenly rose up and made a shot from a diagonal angle twenty feet away from the basket. Then, she went into the basket again. Huang Shuhua defended her, but as the ball entered the net, Huang was called for a foul. Wang Huizhen recovered five points for Southeast, making it twenty-five to twenty-five. The situation suddenly turned into a tie. With two minutes left in the game, the atmosphere was tense, and the whole stadium shouted.

Alas, One Point The outcome of the game was about to be decided in these two minutes. Everyone was flustered and gained nothing. Unfortunately for Southeast, Qin Ruiying, who replaced Lu Xueqin, was suddenly called for a foul. Yang Sen made the free throw. This one point created victory for Liangjiang. However, Southeast's Sun Yuxiu also got a free throw in the last second, but the ball did not go into the net, so she could only sigh in defeat. The game was resolved with a score of twenty-six to twenty-five.

Special Art The performance of both sides, in the cold weather, was so wonderful that it could be called unprecedented for both sides. Liangjiang's forward Chen Rongming was the most agile, flipping over under the basket and tossing the ball backhand, which was indescribably beautiful. Yang Sen was under surveillance, but she was very proud. Southeast's Wang Huizhen stood out, adding a lot of color to the whole team. The tight surveillance of the defenders prevented Liangjiang from entering the basket, which was also a special feature of Southeast.

Executive Committee of the Jiangnan Sports Association 145

Case of Assaulting Referee Chen Jixiang

Decision on Serious Handling Measures

The Jiangnan University Sports Association held an executive committee meeting on the afternoon of the 29th at the Sports Association Advancement, attended by eleven representatives from six schools. The chairman was Rong Qizhao, and the secretary was Peng Wenyu. Four motions were passed, and the situation is recorded as follows:

Attending Representatives

Shen Guoquan, Liu Liangzhan (Jiaotong), Zhang Xinfu (Central), Chen Bingde (Fudan), Shen Kunnan, Tan Tianpei (Daxia), Cao Yu, Yu Hengzhi, Weng Delin (Jinan), Peng Wenyu, Wang Jihuai (Guanghua)

Four Motions 146

(1) Regarding the case of a Fudan student assaulting a referee during a Jiaotong-Fudan football game, it was resolved that: (1) Fudan's right to host various championship games on its own ground would be revoked for one year (effective from the date of the resolution). However, if any games organized by the association are held at Fudan, they must be moved to public venues. (2) The association should express its attitude to the referee on behalf of the association. (3) The association should send a letter to the Fudan authorities to severely punish the student who committed the assault and to apologize to Chen Jixiang and bear medical expenses.

(2) Regarding the motion to limit the qualifications of athletes in the association to university students only (proposed by Shen Guoquan and Zhang Xinfu), it was resolved that it would be reserved for discussion at the next executive committee meeting. (3) Regarding the motion to prohibit formal team members of the schools belonging to the association from participating in any external leagues during a sporting season (proposed by Shen Guoquan and Zhang Xinfu), it was resolved that it would be reserved for discussion at the next executive committee meeting. (4) Jiaotong University's request to hold the spring track and field games and all-around games at the school's track and field field was passed. However, the issue of the date of the meeting and the number of times each person should join the track and field all-around three-item championship was transferred to the standing committees of track and field and all-around for handling.

Lu Shaoji's "Guidance for University and Middle School Entrance Examinations" Becomes Popular 151

Essential Reading for All Young People

Even More Essential Reading for Young People in the Interior

The "Guidance for University Entrance Examinations" and "Guidance for Middle School Entrance Examinations," published by the Qin Fen Bookstore on Fourth Malu Road in Shanghai, were compiled by Mr. Lu Shaoji, director of the Normal Department of Jiangsu Provincial Shanghai Middle School. Mr. Cai Zimin, President of the Academia Sinica, wrote the inscription. Each volume is priced at six jiao. Postage by mail is four fen, and registered mail is six fen. The former book has a total of six chapters, and the latter has a total of seven chapters. Each chapter is divided into sections. According to the level and needs of universities and middle schools, the current situation of universities and middle schools across the country, the standards for selecting schools, the preparation for knowledge, morality, physical fitness, and economics before the entrance examination, the points to note during registration on the examination day, during the written test, during the oral test, during the physical examination, and the preparation for expenses, items, and course selection after admission are all described in detail and practical guidance is provided. It is essential reading for all young people preparing for further studies, and even more so for young people in the interior preparing for further studies. Therefore, since the publication of the two books this summer, many students above middle school in the interior and booksellers have directly written to the bookstore to purchase or wholesale them. Mr. Cao Baomin from Chaoxian County, Anhui, recently wrote to Mr. Lu, saying, "The two books are rich in content and well-organized. Young people in the interior have obtained this guide, and the benefits are immense. They are truly books that benefit the world." The praise and popularity of the two books among people in the interior can be seen from this. The winter vacation is approaching, and new student enrollment for various schools is imminent. It is heard that the bookstore has a limited number of books printed and not much stock left. Anyone who wants to read the two books should purchase them from the bookstore as soon as possible.

Gold Standard Prices Rose for Several Days, but Yesterday Began to Reverse and Fall 152

Spread ··· Fourteen丨Decline Degree ··· Four

The Peak Appears and Immediately Goes Downstream

Central Bank Opens Cash and the Downward Trend is Slightly Checked

A Quick Sketch of the Entire Process Yesterday, the market gold standard price fell because of the external London large bars near and far shrinking by 1.25, New York silver price also fell by 1.25, British-American and American-British exchange rates fell by 1.375, and telegraphic silver price also fell slightly by 1.25. The exchange market did not see any improvement due to the underlying weakness of the large bars (after the close, the United States tended to buy). Therefore, the opening price of the British exchange rate was the same as the previous closing price, while the opening price of the American exchange rate, although slightly tighter than the previous closing price at the beginning, loosened after the opening, and so did the gold standard price. Although the opening jumped to 833.2 taels, rising to 2.4 taels (another new high price), it immediately went downstream. Large households, seeing that the rising path was blocked, became suspicious of each other. Cheng Feng Yong first sold at 818.8 taels, and then the Guangdong group sold off later. Although new prices were frequently seen, there were many buyers at the top of the market, which was also the case yesterday. High prices have been formed, but it is not known who created this market trend. Although the price has slightly gone downstream, it has not fallen too much. Da De Cheng Fu Yu Yu took the lead, and the exchange market also loosened accordingly, falling to 22.5 taels. Fortunately, the Central Bank came as a pillar in the middle stream and continued to open cash, so it turned peaceful, and the people's hearts were still good. Now, the situation of the whole city will be recorded in detail below.

The Morning Market Goes from High to Low The morning opening was affected by the decline in silver prices, so it opened high at 833.2 taels, an increase of 2.5 taels to 2.4 taels compared to the previous close. Fu Yu and others sold slightly, retreating to 2.2 taels. However, at this time, the people's hearts were still good, so the gold price hovered between 2 taels. When Da De Cheng Tian Feng Yong Lai sold, China-Belgium also sold January at 27 yuan, falling to 30.5 taels. Retail investors slightly paid, rising to 1 tael, and the exchange market trended to loosen by 0.0625, which could be settled in January. Fu Yu Heng Yu Qing Fa Yong sold off, and the price went downstream. Helplessly, the internal market of the banks became harder and harder. HSBC issued January American exchange at 125, and Da De Cheng sold fiercely in the market, falling by 8 taels in ten minutes, falling to 25.2 taels. HSBC listed British exchange unchanged, American exchange shrank by 125, Heng Xing Lai entered, and the price began to turn flat. It was also heard that the Central Bank had news of opening cash, so it rose to 7 taels. However, the exchange market was still loose and excessive. March American exchange at 375 could not be sold, and January American exchange at 1875 could be settled. Tian Feng Yong Heng Yu Ri Chang and others sold off, and then fell by more than 3 taels, to 23.5 taels. Yuan Heng bought bars, and the price rose slightly. At this time, Mitsui sold March American exchange at 4375, and the Central Bank continued to open cash. Heng Xing Tong Feng Heng re-entered, pulling 12 taels. Before long, it fell back, and the exchange market also turned flat. January American exchange at 25 was wanted by the bank, so it improved to 6 taels. Finally, after rising and falling by a few cents, it closed at 25.6 taels. Goods were auctioned at 5.5 taels.

The Afternoon Market Gradually Returns to Calm The afternoon opening was slightly smaller, at 25 taels. The market situation was very flat. Yuan Chun slightly paid, and the price rose slightly. The exchange market improved. March American exchange at 2125 could be sold, and people's hearts were upward, rising to 7 taels. Bing Xing Fu Yu sold, and the price gradually became unsustainable. However, China-Belgium wanted February American exchange at 3125. Heng Yu Yi Feng Yong Lai entered, gradually reaching 8.2 taels. Heng Xing sold off in the market, and Heng Yu Qing Fa Yong followed suit. Meng telegraphed that Ana rose. Retail investors sold, and in an instant, it went down by 2.7 taels. However, the exchange market did not drive it. The banks made a deal on April American exchange at 275, which was tighter than in the morning. The gold price rebounded and returned to 8 taels. Heng Xing still sold, and it fell again to 36 taels. The transactions of each company were also scattered. Da De Cheng Lai entered and rose to 7.4 taels. Zhi Feng Yong then exited, and it hovered for half an hour, closing at 26.6 taels at 4:30. Goods were auctioned at 7 taels. It was found that the highest price in the city was 833.4 taels, and the lowest price was 823.5 taels, with a difference of 9.9 taels. As a result, it fell back by 4.1 taels compared to the previous close.

The Opening Price is Mostly Suppressed by Eight Taels The opening price was calculated as 897.2 taels because HSBC listed American exchange shrinking by 124000, which is in line with the gold standard price. According to the closing price, it was suppressed by about 70 yuan, which is 8 taels more than the previous day. The account price for January was 826 taels, the same price for February, and the subsidy was 823 taels.

The Central Bank Continues to Open More Than 600 Bars of Spot Goods The Central Bank continued to open spot goods of about 600 bars, with prices ranging from 24 to 25 taels, which is about 1 tael cheaper than futures. De Cheng Tong Feng Heng Heng Xing and others acted as agents in the market.

The Volume of Transactions is Still Thin The transaction statistics of the whole city show that Fu Yu, Tian Feng Yong, Bing Xing, Da Xing Yong, Chang Sheng Yong, Qing Fa Yong, Hong Xing, etc. were the sellers, while Fu Chang, Zhao Feng Chang, Zhi Feng Yong, Yuan Heng, Feng Yong, Hong Li, Heng Xing, Heng Yu, etc. were the buyers. Except for Heng Xing entering more than 200 bars on behalf of customers, Yi Feng also remained on the sidelines. All the February bars, as of the 29th, totaled 18,900 bars, slightly more than before.

The Extra Red Increase of 7.5 Taels The extra red has been calm for days. The Central Bank is willing to reduce the price and open cash, so the price has slightly risen. The increase is 7.5 taels. There are not many transactions in the market. Silver shops sell slightly, and only Ying Feng Heng enters. Transactions are still less than 100 taels.

Swap Trades Go From Boom to Bust Swap trades have been booming for days. Extremes meet, and yesterday there were very few transactions in the market, because each spot goods company learned that the Central Bank was indeed willing to reduce the price and open cash, which was about 2 taels different from futures. Therefore, although Heng Xing was willing to pay, it did not see the price of the previous day (the multiple parties paid 2.5 taels), and only Ying Feng Heng swapped January to February to Heng Xing at a price of 2 taels, about 105 bars. Year-End Major Summary: Bank of China's Foreign Funds Are Peaceful, and Collection and Settlement Are Tedious 155

This year's commercial market is sluggish, and after the January 28th National Crisis, the market's depression lasted for nearly half a year before it slightly improved in the second half of the year. However, because the financial community was unwilling to lend money as much as possible, the commercial market that wanted to be revitalized but was not, experienced an economic panic. As a result, at the year-end major closing period, there was still no significant transaction. Therefore, this year's total summary situation is far less prosperous than in previous years. However, the market is still peaceful, without any major disturbances, which is fortunate.

Foreign Cent Price is Flat, Transaction is Weak, Silver Rate Follows Old Rules The early market cent price for "foreign cents" was seven qian one fen one li six hao two hu and a half. The afternoon market was unusually sluggish, so transactions were also declining. The "silver discount" was two fen in both the morning and afternoon markets, which was still the same as the previous day's market price. However, the situation was loose, so it was either two fen or white borrowing for days. The silver head adding water had no market yesterday.

In the afternoon market, the buying interest of the same industry was prosperous, so the market price rose madly. The closing price was a huge six qian four fen and a half li higher than the early market, with transactions of 9,000 corners in the early market and 17,000 corners in the afternoon market. The Guangdong minor coin was six qian one fen four li in the early market and five and a half li in the afternoon market. Although the price difference between the two markets was one and a half li, it seemed to be 1.5 li lower than the price in the afternoon market of the previous day. The transaction was 60,000 corners in the early market and 75,000 corners in the afternoon market. Copper coins lengthened by 1,500 wen, to 393,500 thousand wen, with transactions of 40,530 thousand and 500 wen, totaling 10,300 taels.

A Bird's-Eye View of this Month's Standard Yarn and Cotton Delivery 159

A Concise Review from the Beginning to Delivery

Residual Bale Amount of Yarn is 6,700 Bales

Only 1,200 Bales Were Actually Delivered

The Standard Yarn of December was launched in early July at a price of 143-4 taels. Later, due to the bad weather of American cotton and serious insect pests, the market price rose. At the same time, a certain yarn company in the Guangdong group searched for cash in the market, and Standard Yarn Rong Xing purchased it, so the rising wind became more and more fierce. In August, the highest price once reached 157-8 taels. Unexpectedly, the American cotton government estimated twice and fell by more than 100 pounds, and the world cotton market crashed and turned down, with a tendency to be out of control. Standard yarn went straight from 56-7 taels to below 50 taels. The Rong Xing bulls struggled hard, but the trend was such that a single tree could not support the building. Yarn from Shanxi and Hebei sought a way out in Shanghai, and the market has since slumped, hovering at a low peak of 46-7 taels. In the autumn, there is usually an autumn sales development, but this year the domestic harvest is called abundant, but the selling price of agricultural products is meager, and the livelihood of farmers is still poor. Yarn sales are equal to despair, so the accumulation of various yarns in Shanghai is increasing day by day, about 120,000 to 130,000 bales. Therefore, at the beginning of December, the low peak was 138 taels. Then, due to the scarcity of cotton from various sources and the impact of the gold market on foreign cotton, the purchase was not smooth, and there was a short squeeze. The market price suddenly rose, and the tired yarn market suddenly saw vitality. The foreign groups had been quiet for a long time and thought about moving. They took a look at the situation and moved to purchase about 20,000 to 30,000 bales. Standard yarn went out of 40 taels and reached a maximum of 44.6 taels. At the same time, the financial community entered January and exited February and March, making arbitrage transactions, about 7,000 to 8,000 bales. The market situation has been hard in recent months. As a result, the last plate was 142.7 taels, with a residual of 6,700 bales, and the delivery price was 142 taels. Only 1,200 bales were actually delivered, and the rest were self-delivered. The goods were 20-count C採花200 bales, 龍船400 bales, 人鐘 150 bales, 松鶴 450 bales. The brokerage number and bale amount for receiving and delivering goods are listed below.

Residual Amount of Cotton is 26,900 Dan Actual Delivery Counted as 21,000 Dan Goods Aspect Shaanxi Cotton is the Most

The Standard Cotton of December started to be listed in July, at 30 taels 12 qian. Then, due to the change in the weather of American cotton and the spread of insect pests, the American cotton government estimated on August 8 that the production would be reduced, and the market price soared by more than 80 pounds. The market price rose accordingly, and the highest price in August was more than 35 taels. Later, the second American cotton estimate was released on September 8, with a drop of more than 100 pounds. The world cotton market was greatly shocked and plummeted. At the same time, a certain manufacturer estimated that the domestic climate was favorable and cotton production increased, and a large amount of cotton was thrown out in the Standard Cotton market, with the amount accumulating to more than 200,000 dan. Therefore, the market atmosphere was quite precarious, and the lowest peak in November was 30 taels and 005 fen. After the lack of supply from various sources, the climate of Huamian in August and September was not good, and there was too much rain in the north, and the Yellow River burst its banks, and cotton production was greatly damaged. The production was reduced from 10,829,162 dan to 8,094,863 dan, and people were even more nervous. In addition, a part of the cotton saw that a certain manufacturer had thrown out a large amount of cotton, and the position was short on delivery, and the short squeeze became special. The market price has been rising day by day, and the highest price has reached 33 taels and 5 qian and a half. As for the seller, seeing the turbulent situation, the seller searched for and bought more than 10,000 bales of Xihua coarse velvet cotton in Tianjin and came to Shanghai for delivery. When the news was broadcast on the business market, the market situation changed suddenly and fell back by 1 tael. However, several factories were determined to receive the goods, and the coarse velvet cotton had not yet arrived, and the market price gradually went up again, and even reached 2 taels. As a result, the last plate was 32 taels and 7 qian, and the delivery price was 33 taels. The remainder was 26,900 dan, and the actual delivery was 21,000 dan. The most of the goods was Shaanxi cotton, and the most of 火機 was 2,000 dan. The most of the receiving goods was Puyi Factory and Tongdi Company, and the exclusive supplier was Xincheng. The brokerage and brand numbers of the two parties receiving and delivering goods are listed below.

Grain from Down the River, Rice Market Sales Increase Daily 161

(Hu Nan) Yesterday, there were more sources, reaching more than 60 ships. Retail sales were smoother, and urban and rural store customers were actively purchasing because their New Year's store stock was insufficient. 包栈胃 Tianjin Group continued to pour in, selling Tong稻船头念八号, totaling more than 3,000 shi. Therefore, the market conditions soared, Su Tong Group rose by a corner and a half, Chang Group high goods rose by a corner, and Zhongguan goods rose by two corners. As for 南港青角 and other groups, the Zhongguan goods rose by two corners and five cents, and the high goods increased by more than a corner. Early rice also rose by a corner, 變元 rose by two corners. 阴元’s sales went slack due to the wine jug group’s slack sales, and the price only increased by five cents. There was still a lack of 洋杜尖 arrivals, and the price also rose by one corner and five cents. Looking back at the accumulated stock in Puzhong, although it is thick, the inventory has decreased with the recent smooth retail sales. If there are fewer ships arriving in the future and sales continue, then the price is expected to rise.

(Hu Bei) Yesterday, more than 40 ships arrived from down the river. The white粳堆 household still bought, and retail sales were flat. The price was stable. Zhongci increased by nearly a chi. The high goods of 杜埠尖 were scarce, and Zhongci sales were good, and the price was also firm. Yin Yuan arrived in small quantities and sales were active, Bai Yuan and 羊尖 prices increased by about a chi. 薄稻 also increased by a few cents, and the 客尖 had no glory or disgrace.

Spot Flour Demand is Still Strong 162

丨Fufeng Opened to 2 Taels, Exceeding Standard Flour丨

After the standard flour stopped trading, the spot goods still went out extremely smoothly. The closing price for December was 1 tael 5 qian 8 fen, and the closing price for January was 1 tael 9 qian 1 fen. The spot flour asking price was because the 客帮 demand was very strong, and the factories naturally raised the price. It is heard that Fufeng opened to 2 taels (but there is very little spot flour, and it is also difficult to ship from 木街), and Shen Da Huafeng and others opened to 1 tael 9 qian 8 fen, one is already exceeding December, and the other is already equal to the December standard. This kind of situation is really unexpected. (On the 29th, Fu Fu and other factories opened 170,000 bags again, which were handled by the North and South Ocean groups) Therefore, when the January market opens, it is feared that the extreme tightness of the spot goods will continue to be high.

Rice: Customer Price Drops Half a Dollar 163

Fujianese merchants continue to clear stock at lower prices... Small glutinous rice also sees transactions. Yesterday, imported Yuan rice and Xiang rice were sluggish in sales. Due to merchants from the north and south shifting to river-bottom rice, sales came to a standstill. Customer Yuan rice, despite its excellent quality and popularity among local customers, saw customers shifting to river-bottom Du Yuan rice due to the rising prices of Customer Yuan rice since last week, which attracted transporters. In the past two days, as many as five or six thousand bags arrived. Fujianese merchants took the opportunity to depress prices. Yesterday morning, Wuhu Yuan rice opened at a sudden drop of twenty or thirty cents. The price continued to fall in the afternoon, more than fifty cents lower than the opening price a few days ago. Xiang Yuan rice also dropped thirty or forty cents. The general market opened with 150 bags of Hunan machine-milled rice, priced at $9.90. 2,163 bags of Wuhu machine-milled rice opened at $10.03 in the morning, then dropped to $10.01 or $10.02, and further down to $9.90 in the afternoon. Zhongguan cargo dropped to $9.50. With ample stock arriving, the market is expected to remain soft. The market continued to offer 100 bags of old small glutinous rice, which were still cleared by the local market at $7.65, the same as the previous market price.

Sugar Market: New Trend of Qing Sugar Prices Soaring 164

Yesterday, due to the upcoming five-day customs closure and the guild's decision to close the market for two days on January 1st and 2nd, trading at the guild was extremely quiet. Only 200 bags of second-grade granulated white sugar were traded in the afternoon at $15.88875, slightly down by 1.25 cents from the previous day. The remaining stock saw few transactions. Due to strong sales of new Chao Qing sugar in recent days, local prices have soared. According to telegrams, high-quality sugar has risen to $17, equivalent to about $9.30 per picul in Shanghai, exceeding Shanghai's price by twenty or thirty cents, creating a reverse situation. The market is expected to be volatile.
