Memories of a Fragmented Past ㈡ 184

— Shi

Since I was little, I rarely had the opportunity to meet my father. I feared him as if he were a fierce god. So, until now, whenever I imagine his face in my mind, I can't even remember an outline. But once, his face was always vividly present in my heart. The impression was extremely negative. After our family's first bankruptcy, I had just been admitted to middle school. My father, under the severe blow, even struggled with our brothers' tuition fees. My uncle agreed to bear this burden, but my uncle was also a typical miserly rich man. So, on the night before my brother and I entered school, Father called us to his side and asked us about all the fees that should be paid. He allocated the various expenses according to the most stringent policy. We knew that his allocation was not enough, but we didn't dare to speak. My brother was even more afraid of him than I was. Finally, regarding the money for buying bedsheets, I plucked up the courage to stand behind him and said, "At least two sheets should be bought for replacement." This made him angry. He turned his head sharply and glared at me with a ferocious look, saying, "You want to buy a hundred sheets!" This kind of ferocious appearance and voice was always imprinted in my heart afterward. I tried many times to shake off this memory, but I never succeeded, because I believed that perhaps no human father had ever shown such a frighteningly ferocious face to his child.

But my father was an extremely capable man. With the help of my uncle's power, he soon revived his family business. However, like a flash in the pan, it immediately encountered a second, more dangerous storm. After this time, my father could never rise again, and our family gradually fell into the deep abyss of poverty.

Fortunately, when our family could still support it, I decisively left the country and ran to Japan.

Not a day would make me feel at ease. Whenever I thought of my family, that unfortunate family!

In addition to the economic storms, my family was often quarreling. My father, in his most proud moment, married a concubine, which my mother found out about. My mother wanted to commit suicide and become a nun, but we finally restrained her. But this family, from then on, became a repair shop. In the middle of the night, we brothers often woke up from our dreams, trembling with fear, listening to my mother's screams and curses or the sound of things being thrown.

No matter how hard I tried, I couldn't escape this bewilderment. After I had lived in Japan for two years, one night, I had such a dream:

"I seemed to have returned to my unfortunate family again.

The home was two cramped rooms. The room smelled of filth. A broken bed, a square table, two chairs, and nothing else.

My brother was groaning on the bed, his face pale, like a dying man.

My younger brother! That poor child who was suffering from an unhappy family, was crying on the square table.

My father, frowning, wandered around the open space in the room. Mother sat by the bed, screaming and cursing.

Like a flash of sparks, they fought together. I wanted to stop my mother, but she became even more angry and bit me on the arm."

I woke up from my dream with a painful cry. At this time, a faint dawn was appearing in the foreign sky. A child whose emotions were barren actually had tears welling up in his eyes. (End)

Forgetting 1932 185

— Du Heng

Today is the last day of 1932, which means tomorrow is New Year's Day. However, recently, we Chinese people are not celebrating the New Year. This is not entirely because the people's livelihood has been plagued recently, and everything has been destroyed, so that even a 'New Year's Eve dinner' is unaffordable for a family. There are still quite a few people willing to spend three yuan to see Dr. Mei's play. We Chinese people are putting aside the New Year and celebrating the old year. If you try to innovate and buy a pig's head today and prepare to invite the gods, then, 'Are you celebrating the solar New Year?' People who see it will definitely ask you this question in surprise.

The person who asks this question certainly won't feel that he has committed a serious crime of despising government decrees: not to mention anything else, the two words 'solar calendar' are simply misused, he should say 'national calendar'.

This national calendar was originally promoted by our revolutionary government with decisive revolutionary measures. At that time, the effort spent was indeed not small, at least much greater than the effort used this year to deal with the Japanese imperialist armed invasion. When it comes to the facilities and innovations in recent years, this point really has the right to be listed as number one. Unfortunately, this national calendar is probably because it is not a genuine domestic product, so probably at least 300 million out of our 400 million compatriots are still not used to it. For example, when it comes to celebrating the New Year, I am afraid that at least 300 million people are celebrating the old year: as for the New Year, I am afraid that they can't even remember it.

For example, me. Although I may not be so outdated that I can't even remember it, if I weren't holding a pen today to find a topic to write an article, then I'm afraid I would have forgotten this New Year's Eve.

Speaking of forgetting, 1932 was indeed a year in which the Chinese people showed the most forgetfulness. From our respected officials to the lowly servants, almost everyone has forgotten that 1932 was born in the flames of war: compared to this, the matter of whether to celebrate the New Year or not, mentioned earlier, is really insignificant. Really, why should we keep these things in our hearts? The flames of war are far away. Even though science is developed, a cannon that can transmit sound as far as three thousand miles has never been invented. We don't have super-hearing. Naturally, we are left in peace: even if there is a radio to replace super-hearing, all that is heard on the radio is the sound of opera and music, and there is still a peaceful scene in our ears. We are still left in peace, peace and forgetfulness.

Okay, let's forget 1932 along with everything about it. Let it pass quietly, and what awaits us is, of course, a prosperous and peaceful 1933.

Faith in Turbulent Times 186

— Fu Donghua

In turbulent times, there is much faith; in turbulent times, there is no faith. Much faith is equal to no faith. If someone asks me if I have faith, I say yes, yes, yes:

I believe the Earth is round.

I believe the whole is greater than the part, and the part is smaller than the whole.

I believe seven times seven equals forty-nine, and seven plus seven equals fourteen.

I believe all humans die.

I believe you can't have a son without sexual intercourse.

I believe chanting scriptures and spells cannot save the country.

I believe I would rather die than trust myself.

··································

Faith and superstition are originally sisters, so many people mistakenly recognize superstition as faith.

How can belief become superstition?

I have a friend who returned from the United States studying "Leadership Skills" (ＡitofLeadrsh　). He told me, "If the ×× government gives me five hundred yuan every month, I will be superstitious about ××ism." This is truly a golden saying, hitting the nail on the head!

What is known as American "Leadership Skills" is the art of using five hundred yuan, fifty yuan, or even five yuan, five jiao, five fen symbols, to make people superstitious. A leader without followers cannot be a leader. Leaders each lead their followers worth five hundred, fifty, five yuan, five jiao, five fen, and fight with other leaders, and therefore the world is in chaos.

In turbulent times, there is no faith, only the faith of the leader, and the leader's faith is the cause of chaos.

If people each believe in the truth and do not believe in leaders, then the world will be peaceful.

However, these five hundred, fifty, even five yuan, five jiao, five fen are so necessary and reluctant to give up, then is chaos the destiny of mankind! It is said that it lies in education.

(Note: My opinion is roughly the same as Mr. Qi Fan's "Rejecting Geniuses," but I cannot agree with Mr. Qi Fan's "Honoring Ignorance." Because one of the main factors of genius is the ignorance of others.)

Suzhou Impression (Continued) 187

— Zhen Fu

It plays low music, it plucks the faint strings, just this quiet and beautiful place is enough to make people yearn for it. It is the spring in the mountain, it will never flow out of the mountain, of course it can maintain its permanent purity.

After we came out of the Bowl Spring, we went to the mountain. The stone steps on the mountain are cleverly built from the original stones. The mountain road is winding, and occasionally wild flowers and weeds hold onto our clothes, warning us not to move forward; is it that natural scenery is not allowed for people to peep at? Is it afraid of the danger above? But we finally ignored them and bravely moved forward. Strange rocks are everywhere, all seem to have been carved by supernatural craftsmanship, some standing upright, seeming very dignified, some lying down, expressing a different kind of leisure, some wearing green moss coats, some wearing red and green small flowers, some like wounded beasts, with many scars carved on their bodies, making angry shapes. As we advanced, a large rock stood across the road, and we had to lower our heads and pass under it. Some stood towering into the sky, blocking the way, and we had to change direction. At one place, a large rock suddenly split into two, and we had to proceed in the crack, which is the so-called One-Line Sky. Above the mountainside, there are no paths anymore. We climbed over the rocks, clung to the kudzu vines, and after many twists and turns, we finally reached the top of the mountain. On the top of the mountain, we can see the undulating peaks within Suzhou, we can see the faint Taihu Lake, we can see the crisscrossing fields and the orderly houses, as if doing an aerial view. Because we had to hurry to catch the boat to Mudu, unfortunately we couldn't stay long and hurried down the mountain. The maple trees at the foot of the mountain, although only a part of them gradually turned red, the small maple leaves on the ground are already very red, like a child who has just drunk wine, and is so ashamed to see strangers, this is how lovely red it is! This is worth praising and singing. We picked many branches, carried the sun, stepped on the rustling grass, and returned in the nodding of the reeds and the natural songs played by the branches. Below is a poem commemorating Tianping Mountain:

The grotesque rocks are truly frightening, all stationed in Tianping. If Mi Fu came to this mountain, he should bow down every step. It is a pity that the maple leaves are just beginning to turn red, all the spirituality is concentrated here. Diligently pick one branch after another. How can it compare to the red beans, which are the most missed. Tune: Yu Meiren

When we arrived at Mudu, the boat had already left a few minutes ago, only a few minutes. But what else can we do? So we started walking, from Mudu to Suzhou, only twenty-seven miles, it shouldn't be difficult to walk.

The sunset gradually faded, from a white color to a golden color, faintly laid on the ground, grass, and branches. When its light spread to the water surface, part of it was taken away by the sailing boats; part of it laid on the water surface was disturbed by the sound of oars and ripples, stirring into thousands of points of light, shining into people's eyes. We walked with our backs to the sun, along the bank, in this golden world, how happy it is!

We walked to Hengtang, which made us miss Chen Yuanyuan of the late Ming Dynasty. Didn't Wu Meicun tell us clearly, "In a past life, I should have been a lotus picker, with a piece of Hengtang water in front of my door"? Didn't he also tell us, "The double oars of Hengtang fly like wings, where did a rich family forcibly take her away"? We look at this piece of Hengtang碧water, and imagine the situation of Yuanyuan at that time, isn't it enough for us to savor? Let's put together a few sentences as a memorial:

The water of Hengtang碧is as clear as Xu, only remembering the companions washing silk. Suddenly passing by and turning back, the fragrant grass and slanting sun are melancholy in the east of the water. Where are the traces of Yuanyuan's beauty, the maple leaves are cold on the Wu River. May the fragrant soul not return under the moon, the beacon of Shenzhou is still urging the chaos. Tune: Yu Meiren

While we were lingering in Hengtang, the sun was secretly taken away by the shadows of the sails, and carried away by the water flow. The only part we were carrying on our backs was also taken away by the crows returning to their nests. Fortunately, Chang'e's silver lamp has already hung high, so we have turned from the golden sunlight into the world of bell light, allowing us to experience the quiet night world, this is such a fortunate thing! In the starry lights, we smiled and returned to Suzhou.

Shanghai, December 11, 1932

"Watching" and "Escaping" 188

— Shen Gangfu

"Watching" and "escaping" are the two signature moves of the Chinese people.

From marrying a bride, carrying a coffin, copying targets, fighting, to two yellow dogs having sex in the street, it will always stir up some idlers to watch with relish: when there is a big fire, it is even more lively, people rush to watch from all directions, and it is not surprising that people die.

However, if you hear that the fire has burned through the electric wires along the road, a group of people will immediately turn around and run away, showing their ability to escape, which is also inevitable.

In the meantime, there are also clever friends who simply combine "watching" and "escaping" into one, and things become a bit comical, just like during the Shanghai war, when Japanese ronin were showing off their power on North Sichuan Road, a large group of Chinese people were watching, and when the ronin waved their leather whips, the Chinese people ran away while watching.

Even regarding national affairs, the Chinese people are no different: the volunteers are fighting bloody battles in the frozen wilderness outside the Guan, but the people inside the Guan are like watching the Three Iron Roosters, watching how it ends around the stove: once the Japanese army arrives in Shanghai, they are at a loss like dogs without a home, running away with their heads in their hands.

However, although watching a fire from across the river is not a virtue, and standing under a collapsing wall is certainly not the way of a gentleman, how can the land of Chinese etiquette be without gentlemen?

Therefore, someone said: China is going to perish because the Chinese people only know how to "watch", but the Chinese will not become extinct because the Chinese people know how to "escape"!

Year-End Melancholy 189

— Fu

The north wind roars, and the earth returns to spring. This harsh and cold end of winter is about to say goodbye to us.

Walking into the house, looking at the calendar of 1932 on the wall, only a few thin pages are left; walking into the street, the bustling figures and the New Year lanterns are shining in my eyes, startling me, telling me everywhere that it is the end of the year, the end of 1932.

It's strange, people always seem to be busy with farewells at the end of the year. Everyone can't help but have all kinds of emotions, and I'm not very clear about what these emotions contain. Are they reluctant to leave these few remaining days? Are they pinning their hopes on the future New Year? However, theoretically speaking, the latter is more than the former, right? Why still be reluctant to leave this cursed year of 1932? We naturally look forward to the New Year, 1933!

So, you see: aren't the fortune-tellers by the roadside already writing spring couplets with "National Prosperity and People's Peace" and "Good Harvest of the Five Grains"? They are prepared to hang them up together when the New Year comes, which is a sign of hope for the future. This year's financial luck is not good, so everyone hopes to make a fortune next year, this year's official luck is not "prosperous," so everyone hopes to be promoted next year, this year's frequent internal and external troubles, so everyone hopes to turn them into "National Prosperity and People's Peace." In this way, people are all looking forward to the beautiful New Year that is about to come, so why would they be willing to be reluctant to leave these smoggy remaining years?

I don't think so. It's not that I don't have hope, but I often hope for the "future," but as a result, the future makes me fall into the sorrow of disappointment. In the end, the "future" is often not as good as the past. Therefore, if the facts of the past continue like this forever, I will no longer have any hope.

Wasn't everyone eagerly hoping for "last year" at the end of the year before last? However, now let's try to look back at last year, in which aspect has it progressed compared to the year before last? The Northeast was lost, floods were rampant, and famines were caused by crop failures. How can "last year" compare to the year before last? At the end of last year, everyone was grieving over the humiliation of September 18th, wishing to send the unlucky "1931" away as soon as possible, and pinning their hopes on this year. Who knew that as soon as the New Year passed, the Shanghai War would break out, there would be internal strife everywhere, and even a bumper harvest would become a disaster. How can this year compare to last year? Year after year, it gets worse and worse, this is an ironclad fact! If this continues, I really don't have any hope for the future New Year! Therefore, I feel a sense of reluctance towards this dying end of the year.

Another year has passed! Let's not be extravagant about the New Year, let's look back on this year that is about to end from the beginning. December 24, 1932.

The Crossroads of Era and Love 30 190

— Zhang Ziping

I·······I, I······I·······

He said the word "I" several times in succession, and hurriedly circled around again and walked into the fourth alley. Standing at the kitchen door of the last house, waiting for him with a smile, wasn't that petite and lively Zhuo Shuhua?

"Mr. Lin, sorry, it's cold tonight."

"It's okay."

He didn't expect that Zhuo Shuhua would actually reach out her palm to shake his hand. What surprised him was that her hands were as cold as his, and it seemed that his were a little warmer than hers.

He stepped in through the back door. He saw that the kitchen was unusually untidy, with two or three small coal stoves lined up horizontally or vertically. Two women in dirty clothes were washing dishes under the dim electric light.

(14)

Led by Zhuo Shuhua, Haiquan walked into the front building on the upper floor of their house. As soon as he stepped into the room, he suddenly heard a melodious piano sound.

"Do you have a piano at home?"

Haiquan asked Ms. Zhuo.

"No. That's next door."

There was no one in the front building, and there was no cold-proof equipment. He walked in. He still felt a gust of cold air. The furnishings in this room were not as messy and dirty as the kitchen, but there was no special furniture, just ordinary iron beds, ordinary dressing tables, and ordinary tables and chairs. In the middle of the room, there was a large octagonal table with a plate of red melon seeds and a few teacups on it. What caught his attention the most was that there was a telephone next to the dressing table.

"Please sit down, Mr. Lin."

She greeted him to sit down on a chair in front of the octagonal table, and also took a seat in a direction perpendicular to him. Haiquan seemed very restrained sitting in front of Ms. Zhuo, and was speechless for a while, and didn't dare to look up at her. He forced a smile to reduce his awkwardness.

"Mr. Lin, I'm sorry!"

She smiled and brought the melon seed plate to him. He unconsciously pinched a few seeds. At that moment, he took the opportunity to look at Zhuo Shuhua. Her face was full of intimate smiles. He thought, this is really enjoyable. Which of the female students in the school doesn't have a big air, where can you find someone as intimate and polite as her.

"Do you live here?"

Haiquan took the opportunity to ask her.

"··················"

She pondered for a moment before nodding.

"······But, Mr. Lin, don't tell any classmates."

"Zhang Yingkui knows?"

"He doesn't know, I didn't tell him."

Her attitude became serious at this moment, and she restrained her smile.

Jesus's Achievements 191

— Tian Fang

In this era of famine, unemployment, riots, and full of contradictions, the 1.6 billion people around the world who hope that God will save them are celebrating this "Christmas Festival" madly. Indeed, the words in the Bible are very touching, and the turkey is so delicious, and the Christmas village is so beautiful. Even the soldiers in armor, except for the Sichuan generals who do not believe in Jesus, must welcome it for one day. No wonder the Pope of Rome considers it "gratifying." If you don't believe it, please read the news.

Reuters, Rome, 23rd - The governments of Paraguay and Bolivia have notified the Pope of Rome, stating that they are willing to abide by the Pope's proposal for a Christmas truce. Therefore, from 10 pm on Christmas Eve to 10 pm on Christmas night, the war in the Chaco Forest will be suspended. The Pope expressed his gratification at this and hoped that this move could lead to lasting peace between the two countries.

Shells flying, flesh and blood flying away, is originally a terrible sight. If on the "Christmas Festival" and still exchange with artillery fire, wouldn't it be a great scenery. Make people suspect that God no longer cares about things on the ground. How could this be allowed. Therefore, for 波巴.

The 24-hour ceasefire between the two countries, not only God's representative, 丨 the Pope, "expressed gratification," but also me, who is far away and gets no benefits and suffers no hardships, also considers it "gratifying." What I find gratifying is that Jesus, who died more than a thousand years ago and is worshiped by millions of people, still has some slight effect, and it is more than just the damned souls of the two countries that can prolong their remaining lives by one day. What a pity is that the ceasefire time is only "24 hours," and "eternal peace" is just a "hope."

Speaking of the "hope" of "peace," we have been harboring it for a long time. Counting from the first Christmas to today, there have been one thousand nine hundred and thirty-two Christmases. Morning and night, recited in the mouths of pastors, and heard in the ears of the people, it has never seemed to be taken seriously. However, the two words "brotherly love" are still an unfulfilled check, and society seems to have not improved at all compared to the time when Jesus preached two thousand years ago. On the contrary, it has worsened. We still remember when the World War broke out in 1914, didn't the priests of various countries shout "Fight for God" and "Fight for Justice"? But who is fighting for God and who is fighting for justice, we are still at a loss today. Only this batch of damned heroic lives were wasted by ambitious people. This time, more than ten million deaths and 22.34 million yuan (US dollars) in war expenses cannot but call on God to bear part of the consumption responsibility.

Originally, hoping for "peace" can never be achieved by empty words, and "brotherly love" is also quite limited. Catholics will never love Christians, and Baptists will never worship Methodists. This is still believing in the same God. Not to mention the hostility towards pagans. The "Non-Aggression Pact" is just a decoration between countries, and the "Bible" is just a "nonsense." When attacking the weak, it can be used to anesthetize the other party's will, such as "If someone strikes you on the right cheek, offer the left as well," a kind of narcotic. When encountering the strong, it is completely ineffective without politeness. You must fight clearly. Never come. To be tempted by your sweet words. Therefore, after singing "brotherly love" for more than nineteen hundred years, a world-wide bloodshed is still unavoidable, and it is inevitable to enslave people. The reason is that we are trying to achieve the end without understanding the root cause. Therefore, things of slapping oneself in the face are discovered from time to time. Taking a step back, if "justice" is really maintained by the priests, then this group of people who eat "God's rice" are really too irresponsible. They will definitely not be saved after death.

Mussolini said, "Empty words are beautiful, but rifles and cannons are more beautiful." Wilson said, "Justice must be backed by force." People who hope to be saved, listen! Amen.

Science

How to Make Alcohol from Sweet Potatoes and Corn 192

— Shun Ji

(1) How to make alcohol from sweet potatoes: Wash the sweet potatoes carefully, put them on a pot, steam them over water, cut them into thin slices with a knife, and then put them in a stone mortar and mash them with a pestle; when the temperature is slightly lower, about 120 degrees Fahrenheit, mix in the crushed wheat sprouts, and then inject hot water to make it a thin liquid; then wait for it to cool, pour it into a bag made of cotton cloth, squeeze out the sugar juice, and let the sugar juice drip into the barrel; then separately use yeast with fermentation effect, after one day, countless small bubbles will appear on the surface of the sugar juice, and later gradually decrease and cannot float; then pour it into a distiller, steam it into gas, and when it meets cold, it gradually condenses and turns into liquid again, this liquid is called alcohol. (2) How to make alcohol from corn: Peel the corn from the cob, and then put it in a stone mortar and then crush it; add 20 pounds of water and 3-4 pounds of dilute sulfuric acid to every 100 pounds of corn flour, and mix it evenly with a pestle; then put it on a pot and steam it to make it like a paste; after it cools, put it in a mill and grind it, and mix in the crushed wheat sprouts; after a few hours, pour in hot water, then it will turn into a sweet sugar liquid; then filter the sugar liquid in a fine filter, add wine koji made from wheat; after one or two days, the sugar liquid gradually ferments, the small bubbles produced are very numerous at first, and gradually decrease later; when no small bubbles float out, steam it into gas again, and then let it gradually cool down, and after it cools down, it turns into liquid again, this is alcohol. The uses of alcohol: Because alcohol is a fragrant, colorless liquid that is easily soluble in various medicines, it is used as a solvent for manufacturing fake paint, perfume, and iodine tincture. Its nature is easy to burn, and the heat is also strong, so it is used for lighting lamps; and the newly invented alcohol iron is used to iron clothes, and it also has the function of preservation, animals and plants are immersed in alcohol and do not rot for a long time. From this, the function of alcohol can be seen, and its function can also be imagined.

Clerk Communication

Serious and Difficult Problems 193

Mr. Editor:

After reading Mr. Zhang Yiyuan's communication "Falling Ill After Entering a Shop" on the 24th of this month, I feel very sympathetic. The problem he raised is a very important social problem, not a simple trivial matter, so it is worth discussing by everyone. I believe the editor's response to Mr. Zhang cannot satisfy Mr. Zhang's requirements: first, it did not point out the reason why Mr. Zhang is unhealthy; second, the solutions proposed by the editor are not practically feasible for Mr. Zhang.

Mr. Zhang himself said: "Since entering the old-fashioned shop, I have been gradually losing weight involuntarily." Here, I dare to answer: it is because Mr. Zhang has to work more than twelve hours a day, without extra time

Page 18

to rest, resulting in accumulated fatigue and emaciation into illness; naturally, there are also poor treatment and unexpected constraints, such as Mr. Zhang's desire to practice boxing every morning, which is interfered with by the manager, who believes it is unconventional. The rest need not be said.

Indeed, breathing fresh air can strengthen the body. However, Mr. Zhang, in fact, for the sake of his livelihood, for the sake of supporting his family, cannot leave the city or has to struggle desperately for food, or still cannot eat even after being extremely hungry, so how can he talk about moderation in diet! As for what is said about "taking a walk after meals, doing something that makes you happy, and other exercises," only high-class free people have the right to do so. The working-class people who sell their labor, in the current unequal and exploitative society, it is absolutely impossible! If the fundamental problem cannot be solved, singing loudly about the equal importance of physical, moral, and intellectual education, etc., is all in vain.

to the market and then to the countryside. Furthermore, having to rush to shop duties early in the morning, where can the necessary time to breathe fresh air be found; performing calisthenics also requires at least fifteen minutes, where does this fifteen minutes come from? Moreover, his manager and boss would also consider this "unconventional and greatly inappropriate." Nutritional food is certainly a good solution! However, shop assistants receive very little salary each month, and the packed meals they eat on weekdays cannot provide much nutrition, which is also a fact. As for having a balanced diet, it is not something that shop assistants can do; when things get busy.

Only when each worker becomes aware, unites, and fights to win all the rights that they deserve; demands an eight-hour work system, improves treatment, and increases wages, is the correct path, is the fundamental solution, and then other issues can be discussed.

These are my thoughts after reading "Shop Assistants' Communication." I hope the editor will publish it in your column. If the editor thinks it is not possible to publish it, then please pass it on to Mr. Zhang himself. However, I hope it will be published. If there are disagreements, please provide guidance.

The Story of Renting a House 194

— Wen Bing

The reason why the sub-landlord is determined to "rather have a slightly lower rent but not rent to anyone without a family" is because he suffered losses in the past by not considering this point, resulting in a lot of trouble, even dragging on several months of rent, and then disappearing overnight. But once he considered only renting to families, he missed many opportunities. The small room in the pavilion has been vacant for three months. Although many people have come to inquire, they always lacked the sub-landlord's requirement of having a family.

The landlady felt that the house was always vacant, which was a pity, but the sub-landlord's temper was strangely stubborn, and no matter how she tried to persuade him, he would not budge. She, on the other hand, thought that as long as she didn't rent to students wearing long pants again, because the last one who disappeared overnight was a student wearing long pants, there was no need to worry about anything else.

Sure enough, the small room in the pavilion was rented out by the landlady.

Page 19

It was rented to a Suzhou girl. The landlady thought that such a decent girl would not cause any trouble. The sub-landlord knew about it, but shook his head even more.

The girl said she worked in a silk factory in ××, but her appearance didn't look like a worker. She also said that her husband was working in the city, but she often had boyfriends who came to sleep with her at night. All these things made the sub-landlord more and more suspicious and uneasy. The landlady, however, firmly believed that women were generally not as bad as men. As for saying that she might have something improper, that was the case with nine out of ten city women.

A month passed, and everything was peaceful. The landlord relaxed his worries by three or four points. The landlady felt even more that women were indeed not as bad as men.

The second month and the third month also passed peacefully, and the rent was paid in advance, and there was no trouble. The only slight problem was that there were still guests coming and going in the middle of the night.

The girl's words were indeed not a lie. One of her husbands came back from the Japanese, and the landlord was relieved because his condition had been met, and the place was much quieter, especially at night.

But for some reason, the girl has been looking gloomy recently, as if she had something on her mind. However, when her husband was around, there was nothing unusual. The landlady saw her like this and often chatted with her or invited her to eat, because they had been living together for half a year and had a considerable friendship. Sometimes, when the landlady was short of money, she would borrow thirty or fifty dollars from her. The girl never asked her to pay it back and let her pay it back whenever she wanted. When she paid it back, the girl would politely say, "Keep it and use it. I don't need it right now." This made the landlady feel even more that she was indeed not as bad as men and was simply the most reliable woman.

A few days ago, she suddenly said to the landlady, "My mother-in-law died and I need to send some money back. We are very short of money these days. I would like to borrow thirty dollars from you and will pay it back in three days." Coincidentally, the landlady had a sum of money on hand to pay the head landlord's rent and lent it to her immediately.

Three days later, the head landlord came to collect the rent. The landlady went to the small room in the pavilion and saw the girl's husband with a crying face. She comforted him and said, "Sir, your mother has lived to a hundred years old and there is no need to be overly sad." The girl's husband replied in astonishment, "My mother is not dead. It's just that my wife has run away."

"Huh? Your wife ran away? She even borrowed thirty dollars from me..." The landlady was bewildered.

The End of Love 195

— Peng Nian

English, Number 13, has been depressed and unhappy recently, with a worried expression, as if she is very dissatisfied. Her oily black hair has not been combed or washed for several days, and it is as messy as pine needles. Her favorite and most fashionable happiness crepe cheongsam has not been worn for many days. The pair of high-heeled leather shoes with heels smaller than horse hooves, which she usually wears, are not on her exquisite feet today. This is truly an incredible and strange thing. "Is she correcting her extravagant lifestyle? Then, why is she so dejected!" I thought to myself.

The giant wheel of the times keeps turning forward. In a moment of my imagination, another week has passed. That day, when the fish belly white light broke through the dark environment and dawn broke, I was just coming back from a dream. Suddenly, there was a surprising sound outside. After a while, the alley was filled with noise. The morning air, which was as calm as a funeral procession, suddenly became noisy. A group of people were shouting:

"English... something bad... what... English..." At this time, sitting in the quilt, I was disturbed by them from being drowsy to being awake. But I still didn't know what was happening outside, I was just guessing in my heart.

The atmosphere in the alley gradually subsided, and the climax of people's voices gathered at Number 13. So, I entered the path of guessing and wondering about English. "Did English commit suicide? Looking at her appearance these days, maybe..." While I was thinking like this, Old Shi next door hurried in. Gasping for breath, he said to me:

"Old Lou: English, Number 13, hanged herself last night."

"What? What? She hanged herself?" I asked in surprise.

"Why did she commit suicide?" I asked again.

"This is something I don't know. I'm afraid others are guessing the reason for her suicide."

"Did she commit suicide because of love?" I immediately thought of her love affair at ×× University last semester and asked myself this way.

After getting dressed, I rushed to her house. But her family was weeping and wailing, heartbroken. Seeing English's body made me sigh, so I had to stop asking questions. Later, English's father came out and asked a few questions briefly. As expected, it was not beyond my expectations. She committed suicide because of love!

From this, it aroused her past thoughts: She was a student in the Education Department of ×× University. A group of male students, like amorous bees and butterflies, bowed down under her pomegranate skirt. Because of her naturally charming appearance, it was indeed easy to make people drunk and confused, and lure them into the net of love. So, she had the elegant nicknames of "School Flower" and "Plum Blossom Goddess."

With spring in her heart and a lack of reason, she fell in love with Mr. B, a skilled hunter of beauty, not long ago, and then developed a physical relationship. From then on, as the scene unfolded, their emotions and desires reached an extreme climax, simply uncontrollable.

The man finally lacked affection. In their sweet life, Mr. B fell in love with another beautiful young girl, abandoned her for another, and gradually hated her. Later, he simply gave her cold looks and often quarreled. As a result, their love completely went bankrupt. Today, English died a tragic death.

Young students, love is not your bright future, it is a trap of depravity. Please reflect on yourselves quickly! Don't hesitate any longer.

The Wastebasket 196

— Cui

In the past, no matter where you looked, on the main roads of the school, in the woods, in the bamboo fences, or in the thatched pavilions, you could see guys and girls talking, laughing, and telling sweet words, eating sweet candy, sitting side by side, or walking hand in hand. There were some in the morning, and even more in the evening. We won't talk about these, they love me and I love you even more. Let's talk about the stone steps around the water tower and flagpole in Zigong Well. There were always students sitting there chatting nonsense. A was peeling peanuts, and B was sucking hard on his cigarette butt. Some were reading novels, some were singing English songs from the Romance of the Xuan Palace, and some were humming Cantonese tunes. What's even more interesting is the scholar in our class, sitting alone on the desolate lawn reading ancient texts. Now, it's cold, and everything has been swept away by the northwest wind. So the "wastebasket" trick has reappeared before our eyes.

This "wastebasket" is strange. It didn't exist in late summer and early autumn. It only came into being because of the skin-flaying northwest wind. And it all appears on the young ladies. If she is fashionable and has a wealthy family, then she will have to bring two "wastebaskets"! The two pockets on the coat or wool short coat!

How did this name come about? There's a reason:

Miss Zhang may not be our queen, but she is indeed quiet and full of emotion, and she is also good at literature and public speaking. What attracts the most attention is her bright eyes and white teeth, and her teasing glances. However, although she loves to glance, she also implies extreme solemnity. The more solemn, the more she seems worthy of envy! The more she glances, the more she seems lovable! However, everyone only loves her privately. On the path of love, there is no room for a single move, let alone any progress.

It's cold, and she's already wearing a wool short coat. The guys are struggling to find a way to do something. It just so happens that the two pockets on her coat are always open, as if waiting for something to eat. A Cantonese classmate, A-Liang, often sits close to her. So he writes many small notes and throws them into her pocket. Sometimes it's like pitching pots, sometimes it's like a pickpocket sneakily. It's funny to say, our professor of political science seems to have caught a glimpse of it, but Miss Zhang doesn't know anything.

After class, it's time for another class. Miss Zhang runs in again. She doesn't know what to touch in her pocket. She touches several wads of paper, but pulls them out, blushing. When she hasn't finished reading one, she grumbles angrily:

Who is so bored? Are they using my pocket as a "wastebasket"?

At the same time, Miss Li, Miss Lu, ... several other classmates, also found several small wads of paper in their coat pockets. The male students laughed so hard that they leaned back and forth, while the female students were furious.

As a result, everyone forgot that they were supposed to be in class. Fortunately, it was announced that the teacher had taken a leave of absence due to an emergency. Wonderful! Wonderful! The laughter spread from the classroom to outside the classroom.

Debt 197

— Fang Tian

The calendar has been turned to the last few pages, and my mood is not as usual. Recently, I am afraid of seeing terms like "winter sale" in the newspaper, because the word "winter" will make you think of "debt." Moreover, the problem of debt collection is so popular in the world these days. Wasn't the recent French cabinet forced to resign because of debt?

"Poverty" is certainly not a "disease," but "borrowing debt" and "repaying debt" are quite thought-provoking matters. According to the theory of natural selection, when a person is reduced to "nothing left" or "empty pockets," it is their own fault, and they cannot blame others or heaven. They should just retreat and stop eating, so as not to bother the world anymore. But "survival" is the common desire of mankind, and they will never forgive themselves for this. And things are quite different, so there is the so-called "borrowing debt."

"Borrowing debt" is the most difficult thing to do well in human interaction. Written, it seems too impersonal, and oral, it is difficult to say. So, the expression when borrowing debt, although not exactly "panic," is at least a little "vague." I have also borrowed debt. When I open my mouth to tell, I always feel like I am showing my weakness to others. Although it is said that "everyone has times of urgency," my petty bourgeois dignity has not been completely eliminated. I always feel inferior in front of my friends. When I walk out the door, I always breathe a sigh of relief, as if a heavy burden has been lifted. It's not afraid of the cold to say it, but this phenomenon probably only exists with "small poverty." As for borrowing tens of millions, it is certainly done openly and without any shame. At this, I am ashamed of being "outdated."

From borrowing debt, I think of a general fact: "Debt-ridden" is certainly not a respectable thing, but at least it can show your status. Being able to borrow tens of thousands, of course, the more the better! Society will never treat you like a poor person. Only in this depressed situation are there many people who cannot even build a debt tower, which is really pitiful. Don't talk about the farmers and workers at the end of the year, just listen to the bankruptcy sounds in the city.

Novel

Sympathizer (Continued 10) 198

— Zhang Henshui

Meng Guobao said, "Second Sister-in-law, haven't you ever been to town?" Wang Ersao said, "I went once when I was little for a temple fair in the town, but I don't remember it now." Meng Guobao said, "Ah! People in the countryside are so pitiful, they can't eat well, they can't dress well, and they can't see the colorful world." As he said this, he broke off a willow branch and sat on the stump of a willow tree that had fallen into the water. He brushed the surface of the water with the willow branch. Wang Ersao smiled and said, "Mr. Meng always says that he pities us country people. You have a good heart." Meng Guobao smiled and said, "After talking for two days, Second Sister-in-law has shown sympathy for me. Lao Er still doesn't understand." Wang Ersao pressed her clothes with both hands, slightly raising her head, sighed, and said, "Farmers, what do they know." After speaking, she sniffled and lowered her head to wash the clothes.

㈤ The Landlord Came

From this conversation, Wang Ersao felt that Mr. Meng was truly a sympathetic person, and what he said was reasonable. The two of them were separated by a pond corner and talked one sentence at a time. Later, two children leading cows brought the cows to the pond to drink water. Meng Guobao couldn't continue talking, so he got up and left. That night, he came again to continue talking about things in the city. He said that in silk shops, the fabrics could be piled up like mountains, and the shops that sell rouge and powder smelled fragrant even when passing by their doors. In theaters, plays were always performed with sets, and when they sang about mountains, there were real mountains on the stage, and when they sang about water, there was real water on the stage. Wang Ersao was truly enjoying it more and more, and they dispersed late at night. The next morning, Meng Guobao got up and hadn't had breakfast yet. He took some of the remaining gifts he had brought back from the city and wrapped them in a handkerchief, carrying them to Wang Lao Er's house. Just as he reached the door, he saw Wang Ersao carrying a slaughtered chicken: she was about to walk to the pond. Seeing Meng Guobao, she smiled and called out "Mr. Meng," supporting herself against a tree by the roadside, smiling at him. Meng Guobao didn't have much to say, only that perfunctory sentence, "Is Lao Er at home?" Wang Ersao said, "The landlord came, and he's accompanying him in the main room. I was thinking of preparing the chicken and then asking him to invite Mr. Meng for dinner. It's a coincidence that Mr. Meng came. I've fried melon seeds and made hot tea, please come inside and sit down." He heard that Wang Lao Er was accompanying the landlord, and he was a little unwilling to go in, but then he thought that he was here to investigate the rural economic situation, and participating in this conversation between the landlord and the tenant might give him some material, so he smiled at Wang Ersao and said, "I have some small things here to give to Second Sister-in-law, please don't say that I gave them to you, just say that my mother gave them to you, okay?"

Strange News from Abroad

Hollywood's Fortune Teller Talks About Jean Harlow's Future (Part 2) 199

— Lin

Besides Jani Furling, there are also two fortune tellers in Hollywood, Dario and Marlon Nofal. Dario is an astrologer and can also read palms and understand psychology. His observation of Jean Harlow's future is slightly different from Jani Furling's. He said that Jean will definitely become famous in the future, but she will not have happiness. She will marry someone in the film industry within two years, but this marriage will still end in tragedy. After this tragedy, after another two or three years, she will marry someone with the same intelligence as Paul Bern. She loves him, and he submits to her like a tired bird returning to its nest. But the two of them will never be able to achieve complete happiness, because Jean Harlow is born without the joy of marriage. She will continue to work hard in the film industry and achieve great success, but fate will be bumpy, and she will hope for happiness throughout her life. The third fortune teller, Marlon Nofal, is an astronomer who is good at observing the stars and determining good and bad luck. Two weeks before Paul Bern's death, he told the famous director, Griffith, that a big figure in the film industry would soon commit suicide. He said that Paul's suicide was caused by a very subtle and extremely dangerous stellar vibration. He said that Jean Harlow was born on March 3, which belongs to the water element; Paul was born on December 13, which belongs to the fire element; and the star that manages the film industry is Neptune. So Jean and Paul, one belonging to water and the other belonging to fire, were placed together in the same field of Neptune, just like putting water and fire in a bottle. Water and fire will naturally restrain and annihilate each other. This time, of course, water prevailed over fire, and Paul could not escape the path of suicide. Therefore, it seems that Jean and Paul should not have been together in the first place. There was no possibility of them getting along in peace. As for Jean's future, Marlon Nofal firmly believes that Jean will continue to work in the film industry. She will remarry within two years, and she can get some happiness after marriage. At this time, I am afraid that Jean will leave the film industry.

The three predictions mentioned above have their own opinions. We will not know whose prediction is right and whose prediction is wrong until the future. But it is very strange that there is one thing that they all say the same thing, that is, Jean Harlow will remarry within two years. There is also one thing that Jani Furling and Dario agree on, that is, the person Jean marries is probably not someone in the film industry.

, but at least has some relationship with the film industry. As for whether Jean can get happiness after remarrying, the opinions are divided. It is best to remember the predictions of the three of them and see if they come true in two years.

John Barrymore and Marlene Marsh's "Mad Love" is Barrymore's masterpiece. Carldenton continues to show it, and you can still see it on New Year's Day.

Film Review

Review of "Speak Easily" 200

— Yan Nan

In the past two months, the movies shown in various theaters have been dominated by comedies, which also shows the trend of American films.

Buster Keaton's movies have suddenly increased since the prevalence of sound films. Among the veteran comedy stars, no one can compare with him in terms of quantity. The quality is also good. If you don't believe it, you can take a look at his recent "Speak Easily".

The story is about a college professor who was tricked by someone into thinking he had made a fortune. So he resigned and planned to go to Chicago. He arrived in a small village, shook hands with two passengers (vaudeville performers) to say goodbye at the station, but the train left. So he had to find the vaudeville troupe again. Because of his lavish spending, everyone in the troupe flattered him. He also appreciated one of the actresses. With mutual use, he actually became the troupe leader and took everyone to perform on Broadway. At that time, other actresses also tried their best to win him over. With his dull and silly attitude, the performance became a great comedy. At the same time, the huge sum of money he dreamed of actually fell from the sky. The 8,000-foot comedy ends with him kissing the actress.

Keaton's performance is excellent. His iron-like face and very cold attitude, the big moves, are all very pleasing. Jimmy Durante, with the big nose, is working with him for the second time. The reason for the laughter is the opposite. Jimmy is completely happy-go-lucky. Several of the supporting male actors are very good, but the female actors are not as good, and their performances are inevitably over the top.

Movie History Tidbits

The Joke of Talking Pictures 201

— Shi Bin

Ah Bao's mother is playing a phonograph and singing opera; Ah Bao is very curious and asks, "Mom! Is there someone hiding inside?"

When foreign talking pictures first arrived in Shanghai, the villagers suddenly heard sounds coming from the screen. They were baffled and said, "Could there be someone hiding behind the screen talking?"

The first joke is still just a joke, but the second joke, ha ha! has already become a reality! Don't you believe it? I'll tell you, this joke happened in our own country's movie theaters!

A year or two ago! It was during the recession in our country's film industry, and speculative elements in the film industry, seeing the development of Western talking pictures, almost all the business of Shanghai cinemas was taken over by talking pictures! At this time, the Chinese people warmly welcomed talking pictures as a new industry. The heads of small companies were envious and thought about taking advantage of it. They racked their brains and used eye-catching advertisements with "Domestic Talking Pictures" as a facade, saying that they were striving for domestic films! Competing with imported talking pictures! In fact, the trick was exposed. What "Domestic Talking Pictures" were all fiction, just as the villager said: there were people hiding behind the screen! They were lying in wait behind the scenes, reading the subtitles on the screen, just like ordinary conversations! Isn't this the biggest joke in the world?

The above story has indeed become a reality from a joke! Is it true or not? It's just that I'm not willing to reveal the name of this company!

It Wouldn't Hurt to Explore Further 202

— Bing

According to secret reports, in February 1933, two large-scale film companies appeared one after another, and they are currently in the process of very secret organization. The participants are all people in the film industry today with considerable strength, but due to various reasons, they will never reveal their true colors until they reach maturity.

Reader's Opinion

"Don't Know How to Use" and "Don't Know How to Earn" 203

— He

Americans once said about the characteristics of the Chinese nation, "Chinese people in business don't know how to use money, so they don't know how to earn." Indeed, Americans really know how to use money, so they really know how to earn money. Even just looking at the film industry, you can see the correctness of this principle and the reason why American filmmakers succeed and Chinese filmmakers fail.

The article "Paramount's Shanghai War Films" published in this magazine on the 14th said that the company made a profit of more than 2.4 million, which is a good proof of this principle.

Some people say that American films are built on gold, with luxurious furnishings, magnificent sets, skilled actors, glamorous actresses, and their fully displayed red lips and white legs, and everything else. Although many people criticize them for this, American filmmakers have made a lot of money. They really know how to use money, so their money will naturally be earned.

Looking back at our Chinese filmmakers, they are different. Not only do they not know how to use money, but they are also unwilling to use money. Now that they are willing to use money, they still don't know how to use it. Take "Laughing and Crying Fate" by Mingxing as an example. They filmed six episodes, and they were willing to spend money, but because they didn't know how to use it, each episode was worse than the last. If the authorities of "Mingxing Company" knew how to use money, the situation would be different. They would definitely take the money spent on filming six episodes and select the most exciting and meaningful fragments or the essence of the entire book "Laughing and Crying Fate" and film it into one episode, putting the directing, photography, and all the spirit of filming six episodes into one episode, then its results would definitely be very impressive, and it could earn a lot of money.

After Watching "Three Modern Women" 204

— Ai

"Three Modern Women" is indeed a modern film. It clearly says that fine wine, beauties, enjoyment, and leisure are all things of the past, outdated, and not modern. The trend should be popularization and socialization. The story is very ordinary, the directing is still very flexible, the sets are also magnificent, and the photography and lighting are beautiful. Among the products of Lianhua, (except for Humanity) this film shows amazing progress.

What is worth mentioning is the realism of the portrayal of laborers. A modern film that focuses on urban life can also take into account the back of urban prosperity, which is the success of the director.

This film is very suitable for the tastes of all classes, upper, middle, and lower. I hope that modern young people will go and see it, recognize their own position, and learn what is called admirable and enviable "modernity."

Overseas Stardust

Swanson's Children's Education 205

— Sun Nan

Mrs. Swanson now has three children. The oldest is a daughter named Gloria, who is now eleven years old; the second is an adopted son named Joseph, who is now nine years old; the youngest is named Michele, who is also a daughter, and is only six months old.

Since Swanson gave birth to Gloria, she decided that her children would not be allowed to be photographed; not allowed to be publicized; not spoiled; and that all educational supplies should be equipped according to the most beautiful class, giving them the best opportunities; but other than that, they should enter society in the same way as children from ordinary families. She still adheres to her principles to this day, unbreakable. Her children have never been photographed or published in newspapers. Not long ago, a London reporter secretly took a photo of her youngest daughter, and when Swanson found out, she was furious. She is currently filming in London, and she occasionally allows her children to step into the doors of the cinema, but only to make them not completely ignorant of the production aspects of the film. But other than that, she often makes them understand that they are in the same position as children from ordinary families, and also wants to make the students in the school not feel that there is anything different about them.

Zhang Shichuan directed the patriotic blockbuster "Adventures in the War Zone" by Mingxing Company, showing the scene when Hu Die was captured and imprisoned, and the two enemy agents were vying for her attention. This film will be released in the Central Grand Theater on New Year's Day in the solar calendar.

Anecdotes of the Film Industry

The Struggle History of Several Stars (Part Two) 206

— Hong Jun

Constance Bennett lived an unsettled life between New York and Europe as a child. She understood the ways of the world at the age of ten. Her environment was very good, and she lived a wealthy and luxurious life since she was a child. However, when she first entered the film industry, she was despised like Clara Bow, but she did not give in. She was very uninhibited and had experience in the ways of the world, so a twenty-seven-year-old woman occupies an important position among Hollywood stars.

Norma Shearer, who is called Darling of the gods, also had a hard time at first. In the beginning, she couldn't find a position in New York to solve her bread problem. She kept some of the money she earned from work to support her life. She preferred to walk when she went out, saving the fare. After struggling so hard, she was finally recognized for her achievements in silent films. This was not a fluke.

Barbara Stanwyck had it even harder. She was raised in an orphanage. She had a natural voice, and her singing was very moving. At first, she was a dancer, then a singer, and then entered the film industry. She struggled against her predicament for a very long time, and eventually succeeded. She is a star in Hollywood who is known for her courage and魄力.

Joan Crawford's beginning also has an interesting story. When she first arrived in Hollywood, she was an unnoticed minimum dancer; short and fat, wearing ill-fitting clothes, Hollywood was a place where romantic people gathered, how could she not envy their luxurious lives: slowly her ambition sprouted, she developed a desire to be a character, she gradually changed from her inside to her outside: she gradually read books, trimmed her hair, face, and changed to fashionable clothes: from being neglected in the past, she is now enthusiastic, when she married Douglas Fairbanks Jr., she completely broke away from the original Joan Crawford, and created a new and sincere passionate Joan Crawford.
